Cantonese Merchants

Implementing Economic Sanctions Against Japan

People From All Walks of Life Are Participating in the Anti-Japanese Salvation Movement

A Bomb Exploded in Front of a Western Goods Store in Xiguan

Guangzhou Correspondence - Recently, people from all walks of life in the province have started an anti-Japanese movement. All counties and villages have convened anti-Japanese salvation conferences and demonstration parades, and have voluntarily implemented economic sanctions against Japan. There are too many conferences and parades to count. It can be seen from this that the people's hearts have not died. Recently, inspection teams have been set up everywhere in the areas that have implemented economic sanctions against Japan. If any Japanese goods are found entering the country, they will be burned in public. In Guangzhou, anti-Japanese demonstration movements are held every day, and the order is very good. However, those who sell Japanese goods illegally are dealt with severely. The Guangxinglong Chinese and foreign goods store on Tongxing Street in Xiguan was suspected of selling Japanese goods on weekdays. Suddenly, at about 6:00 pm on the 30th, a huge bomb exploded in front of the store, causing a sensation in the city. At first, the citizens thought that the bomb came from the city. After the fire brigade rushed to rescue the injured, they learned that the store had been bombed. A huge hole was pierced in front of the store, and a partner and a customer were injured in the store and sent to the Municipal Hospital for treatment by the fire brigade's rescue team. It was found that the store's partner, Huang Kang, was working at the counter when the bomb exploded, causing injuries to his right foot and leg. The customer, Deng Jingquan, was in the store to buy walnut powder and was about to write down the list when shrapnel flew over and injured both ankles. He immediately fell to the ground. Fortunately, the injuries were not fatal, and he woke up after a while. The police then took the store owner to the Public Security Bureau for questioning. According to him, the store sells miscellaneous Western goods. That day, when a customer came to trade, he suddenly saw a man in black coming to the door and throwing a bomb in, injuring two people. Afterwards, a letter was found in front of the store, signed by the Iron Blood Corps, stating that it was a warning letter. The letter stated that the Japanese soldiers had forcibly occupied the three northeastern provinces and bullied our country too much. Anyone with blood and energy would be outraged, so they have all risen up to implement economic sanctions. This group has previously warned you merchants not to sell Japanese goods. Now you cold-blooded merchants are actually doing the opposite and continuing to trade as usual. We have no choice but to resort to this method. We are giving you a second warning. If you continue to sell Japanese goods, we will definitely destroy all the stores on the street that sell Japanese goods in order to eliminate the traitors. Below is signed "Iron Blood Corps respectfully." After checking, the injured store partner went to the hospital for medication and was not seriously injured and has returned home for treatment. The customer, Deng, was slightly injured and left the hospital on his own the next day. Since this incident, merchants have been warning each other to voluntarily refuse to sell Japanese goods. (September 2nd)

Wuhu Circles' Resistance Against Japan and National Salvation

Japanese Residents Have Left Wuhu for Shanghai

The County Party Headquarters today convened a meeting of all sectors to discuss resistance against Japan. Resolutions included: Party members who purchase Japanese goods will have their party rights suspended; civil servants will be suspended from their duties; the public will be deprived of their civil rights; schools will organize volunteer armies; party members will form suicide squads; civil servants in all agencies will begin military training; banquets and entertainment are prohibited; ten commandments of non-cooperation with Japan are promulgated; and a general meeting of all sectors will be held again at 2 p.m. on the 8th to begin preparing for the establishment of a volunteer army.

The Wuhu educational circles previously planned to send representatives to the capital to petition the National Government, declare the diplomatic policy towards Japan, and request a deadline for the recovery of lost territory in the Northeast. The faculty and students of Jianguo Middle School, Wuhu Guan Middle School, and Rice Industry School have now been designated as representatives, who, together with anti-Japanese association representatives Hong Wenbin and Zhang Yuxiang, will depart immediately.

The County Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of all industry guilds the day before yesterday to organize a committee of the business community to conduct self-inspection of Japanese goods. However, the Party Headquarters did not approve it. The Chamber also formulated nine kinds of slogans for resisting Japan and saving the country and printed tens of thousands of copies, which were posted at the entrances of all commercial establishments in the city.

The issue of rapeseed exports from Wuhu has been discussed in several meetings. Today, another meeting of all sectors was convened at the County Party Headquarters, which resolved that rapeseed exports are entirely supplying raw materials to Japan and should be completely stopped. Japanese residents of Wuhu have completely left Wuhu for Shanghai on the orders of their government. However, Japanese Consul Shibasaki and Shirao remain in Wuhu, and there is one Japanese warship, the Hailong, anchored on the river surface at the customs office. (6th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

A Years-Old Tang Family Murder Case Comes to Light. The County Public Security Bureau, in light of the recent series of theft cases in the urban and rural areas, specially dispatched Inspector Yang Shijie to pay attention to investigation and arrest, and to ensure that the case is solved. Inspector Yang received a report from an informant yesterday that a known thief, Shen Shaoqing, was hiding in the west of Dakura Bridge. Yang recalled the assassination of Tang Zhikui, the owner of Tang Helong Oil and Sesame Store, in September of last year, which was widely suspected to have been committed by Shen Shaoqing, because Shen disappeared after the Tang family murder case. The unsolved case has remained unsolved to this day. Yesterday (6th) afternoon, Yang led detectives to follow the trail and arrest Shen, and recovered a package of stolen goods, which were taken to the bureau for temporary detention. A preliminary interrogation was scheduled for today. According to Shen Shaoqing, the murder of Tang Zhikui, the owner of Tang Helong Oil and Sesame Store, at 2:05 a.m. on September 5 of last year, was done by me and two unnamed people. However, the case was initiated by Tang Zhikui's son, Da Guan. The two unnamed people were also called by Da Guan. We negotiated at the Bailongtan Opium Den before we took action. That night, Da Guan arrived home first. The three of us went west from Xiaodai towards the back door of the Tang family. I pried open the door, and the two unnamed people went inside and killed Tang. I was keeping watch at the waist door. When the wind called for help, the three of us escaped along the original route. When the official questioned why you were willing to help without any benefit, Shen Shaoqing confessed that there was an iron box in Tang Zhikui's bedroom containing more than a thousand yuan in banknotes. After killing Tang, Da Guan allowed us to take whatever we wanted. Unexpectedly, people got up and called for help, and we did not have time to take the banknotes. He also admitted to the theft cases involving the Zhang family outside the city. Tang Zhikui died a tragic death. Now, more than a year later, the murderer has been arrested. It can be said that the net of heaven is vast, and no one can escape.

At the beginning of the department's courses, anti-Japanese national salvation teaching materials were compiled. The ambition of Japan's invasion policy and its causes and consequences, as well as the methods for the people to deal with it, were described in extremely precise terms, and questions were raised everywhere to inspire education. The full text is about 40,000 words. All correspondence students, past and present, will be sent a copy. The department has received many requests from various places to recommend participants and has specially rescheduled the opening of classes to October 15. Applications can still be made before October. Graduates will be informed by letter to the Education Bureau to be assigned to primary school teacher positions as soon as possible.

Municipal Education Bureau Notifies Schools Not to Easily Believe Rumors

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued Notification No. 56 to all schools regarding not easily believing rumors and taking leave without authorization: It has been found that some schools in the city intend to suspend classes temporarily due to rumors outside. The local area in the city is quiet and normal, and schools at all levels should attend classes as usual. Do not easily believe rumors and take leave without authorization, causing more disturbances. This notice is hereby issued for compliance. Xu Peihuang, Director of the Bureau.

Universities Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday

Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Committee Tao Baichuan Attended the Meeting to Dispel Rumors

(Shanghai News Agency) The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of students from various universities in the city held the 12th emergency meeting of the executive committee at the Xiaonanmen Youth Propaganda Group at 9 a.m. yesterday. The situation was extremely tense. The situation is recorded below.

Executive Directors Present: Li Chunsen from the College of Political Science and Law, Hu Wenquan from Datong University, Ping Zuren from Jinan University, Chen Yuejiang from the Sino-French Institute of Technology, Zhu Youxian from Guanghua University, Zhang Taosong from the Law School, Xu Guanbin from Daxia University, He Jingyuan from China Public School, Li Yuanzhang from Fudan University, Gu Jiwu from Jiangnan College, and other executive directors from more than ten schools attended. Tao Baichuan, representative of the Municipal Party Committee, attended the meeting to provide guidance.

Meeting Situation: The temporary chairman was Li Yuanzhang, and the recorder was Li Chunsen. After performing the ceremony, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. Tao Baichuan, representative of the Municipal Party Committee, reported the situation of Anning in Shanghai.

Party Committee Report: Standing Committee Member Tao said that the arrival of the Japanese fleet in Shanghai has made people in the Zhabei Gaochang Temple area extremely volatile in the past two days. However, based on the facts today and referring to the news from the party, government, and military, Shanghai, due to its location and other relations, the Japanese army has no possibility of occupying it. The Japanese army has had a twenty-year plan to invade Shenyang, so it can carry out its ambitions arbitrarily and arbitrarily in the Northeast. It would not dare to make a calculated demonstration here. Regarding the people, they should save meaningless waste, such as posting slogans, parades, and other superficial work, which can easily be used as an excuse by the Japanese. The municipal government and the Public Security Bureau are actively planning to avoid this kind of meaningless action and do practical anti-Japanese national salvation work. The party, government, and military guide the people to carry out anti-Japanese movements on the right track in order to obtain the most effective results. People have been extremely panicked in the past two days. The reason is that a poster with shapes and colors was posted on the wall between Qiujiang Road and North Sichuan Road, depicting the brutal killing of the people in the Northeast by the violent sun and the way the Chinese should deal with it. The Japanese residents were quite touched by it and telegraphed the Japanese government to send warships to Shanghai to protect the Japanese residents. The Japanese newspaper took the opportunity to spread rumors, causing great panic among the Chinese people. Regarding the Northeast incident, the League of Nations has sent the Spanish Consul General in Shanghai to conduct an on-site investigation to see whether the Japanese army can withdraw to its original defense before the 14th. The diplomatic method is like this, but the Japanese army intends to permanently occupy the Northeast, so it sends warships to China to provoke and create the only excuse. Under this situation, the people should try their best to avoid a frivolous move. Of course, China's own strength is not enough in diplomacy, and its military preparedness is not as good as Japan's. Therefore, it must devote itself to international propaganda and tell the details of the violent Japanese invasion of China to countries that can be approached. The municipal party and government agencies have reported to the consuls of various countries stationed in Shanghai to make it clear that the Chinese people are completely fighting for peace to save China. The high morale of the people now is a legitimate expression. Because foreigners rarely read Chinese newspapers and only know news that is unfavorable to China, this kind of propaganda work is very important. As for preparations, China, of course, cannot rely solely on foreigners. The important municipal military and political agencies have made considerable preparations and are making proper defenses to reassure people. There is no need to deeply believe in the rumors that are unfavorable to Shanghai. There are also detailed answers to the issues of the Student Federation sending representatives to request the issuance of firearms, hiring instructors, and having half-day classes and half-day military training in various schools.

Key Resolutions: (1) The representative of the Sino-French Institute of Technology reported that a conflict had occurred with the school authorities due to the issue of suspension of classes. What should the association do? It was resolved that the association should send a representative from Jiangnan College, Gu Jiwu, to the Sino-French Institute of Technology to explain the main points of the association's resolution. (2) The association should send representatives to attend the joint meeting of university presidents yesterday to explain the main points of the Student Federation's resolution in order to facilitate the association's progress. It was resolved that the association should send two representatives from Guanghua College of Political Science and Law to attend. (3) How should the issue of the people who are working hard for the anti-Japanese national salvation work in various schools being absent from classes due to work be resolved? It was resolved that the representatives attending the university presidents' meeting should explain as an attachment that it should not be regarded as absence from classes and should send a letter to the school authorities. (4) The travel expenses for the representatives going to Beijing to request the government to allocate firearms. It was resolved that each person should be allocated 20 yuan by the association and reported and reimbursed upon returning to Shanghai. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Fudan University Officially Resumes Classes Today

To Reassure the People of Jiangwan

Fudan University in Jiangwan has been greatly frightened by rumors from the outside in the past two days, so that students throughout the school are unusually alarmed and have no intention of attending classes. More than 100 people have already asked for leave to return to their hometowns. Therefore, after discussion by the school authorities, it was decided to suspend classes for one day yesterday. Now, because the important party and government agencies in the city have tried their best to dispel rumors and the Zhabei area is as quiet as before, the school will officially resume classes from today. Those who do not attend will be considered absent.

Illness of Two Athletes from Jinan University

Zhuang Shihong and Zeng Rongzhong

Recently, two famous athletes from Jinan University have been seriously ill. One is Zhuang Shihong, who became ill due to the national salvation movement, which was too stimulating for a while. He is now being treated by a doctor and has reported that he is no longer using medicine. The other is Zeng Rongzhong, who suddenly vomited blood after participating in the 400-meter race at the Municipal Games, accounting for one or two liters. He is in critical condition and is seeking treatment at the Red Cross Hospital. The doctor said that he had exercised too vigorously, his blood vessels had ruptured, and he had lost too much blood. A classmate has borrowed blood to supplement him, but he has not yet been out of danger.

Amidst the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement, the Malayan Football Team Defeats the Western Team

=Superior in Spirit and Skill丨Five Games, Four Victories=

=Champion Western Team Meets Formidable Opponent丨Entire Army Collapses in Second Half=

丨Await Tomorrow and See the Efforts of the Chinese Team丨

丨Scheduled to Play Against Jinan University Team on the 13th丨

The Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team, gathering the essence of overseas Chinese players from the Malayan Federation, braved the winds and waves to return to the country to participate in the National Games. Contrary to their wishes, they led the team to fight in Hong Kong and Shanghai, so that compatriots at home, who admired their fame but had no way to see their style, could have a true understanding. In Hong Kong, they played three games, winning two and losing one, leaving a good impression that has long been etched in the hearts and minds of the people of Hong Kong.

Charity Match丨Crowds Gather

丨Joyfully Witnessing the Triumphant Return of Overseas Chinese丨

The Chinese National Sports Association sent a special telegram inviting the team to Shanghai for a charity match for disaster relief. Yesterday, the heavens smiled, releasing light from the cloudy rain. A Sino-Western charity match was thus realized at the Chinese baseball field. Amidst the national crisis, hearing that our compatriots had come from thousands of miles away, these outstanding warriors will surely promote our national prestige on the football field. At one point, crowds gathered to participate in this grand event, benefiting the disaster victims and satisfying their eyes. The intention was excellent. In the seventy-minute battle, it was joyful to see the Malayan Overseas Chinese fight their way out of hardship, turning defeat into victory, and finally returning triumphantly. The ticket revenue from this event was 601 one-yuan tickets and 4,652 six-jiao tickets.

Gathering of Heroes丨Great Battle with the Western Team

丨Qiu, the Center Forward, Has Superb Skills丨

The Malayan team's players are well-organized and have outstanding skills. It is a grand gathering of overseas Chinese heroes. In the great battle with the Western team, they won five to four, which is a natural outcome where the superior triumphs and the inferior is defeated. Among the five forwards, Qiu Yongyuan, the center forward, was the most outstanding. He excelled in heading and kicking, running fast and passing quickly. Left inside forward Guan Shunde from the left wing, Li Wenjie, was skilled in cooperation and good at shooting. He would stop whenever there was an opportunity and always make progress. Right inside forward Ruan Guoying also did his best. Right wing Chen Meian, who was not originally a regular player, performed slightly weaker. The center backs Deng Yuehan and Cai Wenli were extraordinarily active, supporting the attack and defending when retreating. They were remarkable. Xu Yahui was light and agile, but he could not stop the activities of the opponent's Huo Gengsheng. The veteran Yu Weihua, who was once famous, still has skills, but lacks agility and has more toughness. He was more than enough to fight against the iron man Turner. Qin Yuanlian was majestic and awe-inspiring, like Jiang Taigong being present and having no taboos. Goalkeeper Liu Jinrong had both flaws and strengths, but he was also a first-class player.

Deng Yafa

Yu Zhuohua (Leader)　Ruan Guoying

When the Strong Meet丨Champion Fails

丨The Momentum Was Loud at the Start丨

In the seventy-minute battle, the Western team was very loud in the first fifteen minutes, sweeping and attacking directly, with no one else in sight. In two minutes, they broke through the defense and scored. They continued to attack from the left and right. After fifteen minutes, the situation changed abruptly. The two sides came and went, with equal effort. By the second half, the entire army was exhausted, collapsing again and being controlled by others. The goalpost had a spirit and cleared the danger several times for them. Otherwise, there would have been a greater difference in the score. Huo Gengsheng was the most dangerous person in the entire team. The goalkeeper also performed very well. Except for the fourth goal, the rest were not his fault. In addition, everyone else performed well, but they were not as tough as they were at the beginning. That was the reason for the failure. If the field was dry, both teams would have performed better.

One to Zero丨Lost Momentum at the Start

丨Huo Gengsheng Succeeded with One Kick丨

The two armies arrived, waiting for the referee to give the order. They could not find a suitable person temporarily. After a long time, Secretary Zhou Jiaqi volunteered to serve the ball. Malaya kicked off, but the ball went into the hands of the opponent. The opponent almost used a free kick, forcing a corner kick. Turner headed the ball, and it fell between the two defenders. Huo Gengsheng, as if divinely assisted, raised his foot and attacked the goal directly, scoring a goal. The score of one to zero was created in two minutes.

One to One丨Captain Achieves Merit

丨Malaya's Vigor Burst Forth丨

After the Western team won a goal, they stepped up their work. The situation changed abruptly, and the situation was bad. Although the Malayan forwards advanced from time to time, they stopped halfway. After fifteen minutes, things turned around. The inside defense was strengthened, and the forwards were effective. The Western team's goal was in a bad situation. Once, a successful offside was not counted. Captain Ruan received a pass from the left wing and headed the ball into the goal, making the score one to one.

Two to One丨Turner Gets the Ball

丨Western Team Takes the Lead in the First Half丨

After that, Malaya continued to attack with all their might, but it was not successful. Qiu, the center forward, was like a giant, and his technique seemed to be above Dai Linjing in Shanghai and Feng Jingxiang in Hong Kong. Zha Xu had no way to deal with him. Twice he broke through the defense alone, but failed. Another time, the left and right wings shot together, but the goalpost blocked them. There was nothing they could do. Under a good situation, Turner accidentally got a ball, raised his foot and kicked it into the net. In the first half, the Western team took a 2-1 lead.

Two to Two丨The Entire Field Was Surprised

丨Showed Their Skills in Two Minutes丨

In the second half, Qiu, the center forward, led the entire army in a mighty manner, coming from all directions. The ball went from the center to the left, and the left wing picked it up in the middle. The goalkeeper扑地救之, but could not stop it. The ball crossed in front of the goal, and right inside forward Ruan Guoying kicked it with his foot, scoring a goal. In two minutes, the score became two to two. The entire field was surprised.

Three to Two丨Malaya Turns Around

丨Qiu, the Center Forward, Has Excellent Heading Skills丨

The Western team was active for a while, and Huo Gengsheng took the opportunity to attack the goal again. The inside was empty, but fortunately, the goalkeeper saved it in time, averting the danger. After surviving a great disaster, there must be good fortune. Sure enough, within ten minutes, under Malaya's constant attacks, Qiu, the center forward, suddenly rushed forward and scored from the right again. Qiu, the center forward, headed the ball into the goal, cleanly and beautifully. It was not easy. Three to two, Malaya turned around from then on.

Three to Three丨Western Team Rises Again

丨Internal Emptiness in the Midst of Busyness丨

Malaya's left wing, Li Wenjie, was injured and left the field for rest, reducing their strength. Huo Gengsheng was active again. The goalkeeper pushed the ball backwards. Qiu, the center forward, skillfully avoided several people and passed the ball to the center. Left inside forward Guan Shunde hit the goalpost, which was very unfortunate. In the midst of busyness, Malaya's inside was empty. After three or four passes, the Western team's Jieke caught up and kicked the ball in. The score between the two teams was tied again at three to three.

Malayan Football Team (Photo by this newspaper) ○ Leader Yu Zhuohua　Captain Ruan Guoying

Five to Three丨Malaya Wins Continuously

丨Won Two Goals in Ten Minutes丨

In the next ten minutes, Malaya won continuously, scoring two goals and securing the victory. The first of the two goals was scored by Ruan Guoying, thanks to the support of right wing Chen Meian. The second goal was the fault of the Western team's goalkeeper's haste. With a ball in hand, he threw it away. Qiu, the center forward, reaped the benefits and took the lead with five to three.

Five to Four丨Success and Return

丨Welcome Banquet and Tour of the City丨

The Western team was indeed fearsome. In a bad environment, they fought unceasingly. With a slight decision, they used a corner kick, and Huo Gengsheng broke through the defense again. In the end, five to four, Malaya won. At 7 p.m. that night, the Association held a welcome banquet at the Jinling Restaurant. After the banquet, the entire team toured the city.

City Chamber of Commerce Asks to Promote National Salvation

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association

Summary of the Sixth Standing Committee Meeting

The City Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association convened the sixth Standing Committee meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce meeting room at 1 p.m. yesterday. Committee members Wang Xiaolai, Hu Shuhua, Lin Kanghou, Fu Dewei, Chen Tingrui, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Yansong, etc. attended. Chairman Fu Dewei, Secretary Yi Xian, Zhao Shusheng. The following important cases were resolved: (1) The Paper Industry Association wrote to request that the old Japanese goods stored in various industries be handled in the same way as India's boycott of British cloth, that the industry associations designate warehouses to be responsible for centralized storage, and that they be sold publicly on a regular basis. All expenses should be shared from the proceeds of the goods, and the remaining money should be returned to the owners. The case for discussion. It was resolved that all Japanese goods should be temporarily sealed up and then a method should be determined. (2) Regarding the association's mistakenly confiscated non-Japanese goods, the case for exempting the insurance fee was put to a public vote and it was resolved to pass it. (3) Cheng Fengxiang wrote that on the 1st of this month, Chen Jinghua visited a friend at Zhenkang & Co. and was arrested by the inspection team of your association because he was considered a Wufu accountant. The case of asking for his release, it was decided to release him on bail. (4) The Economic Committee suggested that the association's operating expenses be notified to the City Chamber of Commerce to solicit donations from various industry associations according to their levels. The levels are as follows: 2,000 yuan, 1,500 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 500 yuan. The case for review and handling, it was resolved to write to the City Chamber of Commerce and various groups to solicit donations separately. (5) The Storage Department presented the case that the confiscated goods stored in Xiangfeng Factory were not allowed to be retrieved, please review and indicate. It was resolved to investigate the case and pay the supplementary fund. (6) It was reported that a certain bank issued 350,000 taels of banknotes to assist foreign firms and maintain transactions. The case for review, it was resolved to send a letter of warning.

City Chamber of Commerce Notice to All Industries to Promote National Salvation

The City Chamber of Commerce announced: Greetings. On the 4th of this month, we received Official Letter No. 343 from the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party, stating that the Publicity Department of the Chamber had submitted a memorandum regarding the fourth item of the expanded publicity conference, which discussed the issue of resisting Japan and saving the nation. This item was a request from the Chamber to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to notify all businesses in the city to affix anti-Japanese slogans to their display windows. The 13th standing committee meeting of the Chamber resolved to send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to handle the matter accordingly. On the same day, we also received a letter from the Shanghai University Students' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation, which the Chamber unanimously resolved that all businesses must include anti-Japanese slogans in their various commercial advertisements to promote national salvation in a cost-effective manner. Please investigate and handle this matter accordingly.

The above two resolutions are intended to arouse the national salvation sentiment of the people, so that they are awakened at any time and place and by whatever they see. We should handle them one by one to help the people increase their enthusiasm for national salvation. We hereby send this letter to notify you and request that you start handling the matter immediately. For industries with associations, the various slogans to be used should be properly drafted and determined by the association and issued to the respective industries for affixing. For stores without associations, they should carefully consider and draft appropriate slogans, generally aiming for easy understanding by the public.

Women's Relief Association Telegrams

Petitioning the Central Government to Promote Peaceful Unification

Petitioning the Municipal Government to Substantially Promote Domestic Goods

Urging Women Nationwide Not to Use Japanese Goods

The Municipal Women's Relief Association convened women from all walks of life in the city at the public sports field on the day before yesterday (the 4th) to hold an anti-Japanese national salvation rally. The important telegrams issued by the rally are recorded as follows:

Petition to the Central Government: Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, National Government, respectfully. The Japanese troops have invaded the Northeast, repeatedly capturing famous cities. The situation is critical. All comrades of our party are filled with grief and indignation. The whole country unanimously advocates declaring war on Japan. However, the generals in the Northeast still hold on to the policy of non-resistance, and the diplomatic authorities are seeking help from the League of Nations. This policy is incomprehensible. Peaceful unification of our country is not just empty talk. We must abandon past grievances, truly unite, and then we can talk about peaceful unification. As for seeking help from the League of Nations, the countries in the League each have their own interests. How can they offend Japan to help our country? Moreover, the League of Nations has long lost its sense of justice. Otherwise, Korea could have survived on its own, and India could have become independent. Therefore, the League of Nations is not reliable. From now on, in order to ensure our own survival, we must achieve peaceful unification and concentrate the military power of the whole country to resist foreign aggression and alleviate national disasters. We earnestly present our petition, awaiting orders. (Omitted below)

Petition to the Municipal Government: (Omitted above) Since the violent Japanese invasion and occupation of various parts of the Northeast, the news has spread, and all compatriots across the country are filled with anger. Our association leads the people and cannot remain silent. However, the people are poor and the country is weak, and it is difficult to compete with force for a while. After much consideration, the only way to cut off the enemy's lifeline is to boycott enemy goods. Therefore, on October 4th, we held a citywide women's anti-Japanese national salvation rally at the public sports field. At the rally, it was decided to prepare for the establishment of both domestic goods and Japanese goods exhibition halls. The halls will also have a domestic goods introduction agency to instruct the citizens to understand what kinds of domestic goods can be compared to Japanese goods and what kinds of domestic goods can replace Japanese goods. The prices are cheap and the quality is good, and we can also provide agency services at prices lower than the market price. If we intensify our efforts in this way, domestic goods will naturally be able to drive out the position occupied by Japanese goods. On the one hand, we will also persuade the factories to carefully study and imitate all the goods that we lack. However, we must calculate the current small profits, so that the day domestic goods are completed will be the day the boycott of Japanese goods succeeds. In addition, we will organize a propaganda team to specialize in open-air speeches so that everyone can work to resist Japan regularly, in order to achieve the goal of the Japanese army withdrawing from Chinese territory and compensating for losses. The resolution was passed on the spot and unanimously approved. We should present the resolutions of the meeting in writing for your review and approval, and request that you order the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to follow them together to achieve practical results. (Omitted below) Another letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the content is roughly the same. (Omitted)

Telegram to the Whole Country: All female compatriots across the country, The Japanese army violently occupied the eastern provinces, massacred compatriots, and caused countless property losses. It is heartbreaking. The Japanese troops have recently become even more aggressive, eyeing Tianjin and Ping, and even Nanjing and Shanghai. At this critical moment of life and death, how can we, female compatriots across the country, sit and wait for death? We earnestly present our petition, awaiting orders.

Shipping News in the Anti-Japanese Voice

Barges Strike: Since the boycott of Japanese goods, Chinese barges have no longer transported Japanese goods. Japanese trading companies in this port, such as Mitsui, International, and Toyo Cotton Spinning Co., Ltd., all use their own cargo barges for transportation. Therefore, Japanese goods can still be loaded on British ships for export. Now, with the outbreak of the anti-Japanese incident, more than 40 cargo barges belonging to Mitsui, International, and Toyo Cotton Spinning have unanimously and voluntarily gone on strike. The boatmen have united and decided not to carry goods for Japanese merchants anymore. The only means of transportation that the Japanese rely on has now completely stopped.

Shantou Rejects Ships: After Hong Kong refused Japanese ships and refused to load and unload Japanese goods, 20,000 tons of Japanese goods were stockpiled in Hong Kong warehouses. Yesterday, the shipping companies received a telegram from Shantou, saying that the port would take the same approach as Hong Kong. The dock workers will not work for Japanese ships. The Nisshin Steamship Company has ordered the Nanhua to stop going to Shantou.

Overseas Chinese Return Home: Yesterday, more than 100 overseas Chinese returned home from Tokyo, Osaka, Kobe, Nagoya, and other ports. Most of them are engaged in the restaurant business, kimono merchants, and barbers.

The Postal Workers' Anti-Japanese Association Held a Regular Meeting Yesterday

Proposed that the Central Government Implement a Conscription System

Volunteer Corps Training to Be Held on Schedule

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps organized by Shanghai postal workers will begin training on the 11th of this month, held in both the north and south of the city. It is reported that instructors have been hired for both locations. Due to the different working hours of the postal workers, the training time in both locations will be from 9:00 to 10:00 in the morning and from 3:00 to 4:00 in the afternoon, in separate shifts. The association held a regular meeting of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association at the Postal Workers' Club at 4:00 p.m. yesterday and resolved many important cases. The main points are extracted as follows: (1) Propose that the central government implement a conscription system. (2) Methods for collecting anti-Japanese national salvation funds: All postal workers will donate 10% of their monthly salary, collected in October and November. The estimated collection for October is more than 10,000 yuan.

The Anti-Japanese Association Detains Xue Fuji

Great China Rubber Factory

Caught Smuggling Japanese Goods

The Great China Rubber Factory specializes in using Japanese raw materials and applying a little bit of labor to make galoshes and sell them as domestic goods. Therefore, it has made huge profits of more than one million in a short period of time. Yesterday, someone reported the factory to the Anti-Japanese Association, which sent personnel to conduct on-site inspections. It was found that all the raw materials of the factory, such as rubber powder and lining powder, were inferior Japanese goods. The manager of the factory, Xue Fuji, was immediately detained, along with the account books and documents, and escorted back to the association. More than 20 warehouses of the factory's inventory were sealed up, pending a meeting for disposition.

Anti-Japanese Work in Various Sectors

Pudong Seizes a Large Batch of Japanese Goods: The Pudong Inspection Office of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association received a tip-off yesterday, saying that a large batch of Japanese goods was about to be transported for export at the Dalai Wharf in Bailianjingkou, Pudong. The office immediately ordered the inspection team leader, Cao Jinhua, to lead the entire team of inspectors to the reported location. After searching and detaining the goods, a barge numbered 10223 in the Huangpu River was found to be loaded with a large batch of bleaching powder, totaling more than 800 boxes. The boxes were stamped with MN, confirming that they were completely Japanese goods. The owner of the goods fled upon hearing the news. The goods were immediately detained in the warehouse and reported for the record. It is also reported that the inspection team leader, Cao Jinhua, was bravely stepping forward to inspect the goods when more than 100 boxes fell down, injuring his foot.

Chinese and Foreign General Merchandise Industry Establishes Inspection Team: The preparatory committee of the Chinese and Foreign General Merchandise Industry Association established a Japanese Goods Inspection Team the day before yesterday. The temporary chairman of the team, Cheng Yujie, reported the general rules of the inspection team. Shi Hutao was elected as the team leader and concurrently as the investigation committee member, Cheng Yujie as the publicity committee member, Cao Yifeng as the review committee member, Wang Pingyuan as the discipline committee member, and Teng Guoliang as the inspection committee member. The inspection work will begin immediately.

Silk and Satin Industry Representatives Meeting: The Silk and Satin Industry Association held a temporary meeting of member representatives the day before yesterday. More than 150 representatives attended. Chairman Wang Yansong presided over the meeting. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Organize a Japanese goods inspection team. Resolution: Passed in principle. (2) Organize a national salvation volunteer army. Resolution: The association does not need to organize independently. It should immediately notify the industry that those who are willing to serve in the volunteer army can directly register with the volunteer army organization office of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. (3) Negotiate and agree on wording for not buying or selling Japanese goods and engrave a seal to be printed on invoices as a warning. Resolution: Engrave a seal with the words "The silk and satin industry jointly agrees to sever economic ties with Japan and will never buy or sell Japanese goods," and notify all members to comply. (4) Propose to send telegrams to silk industry associations in various places to jointly organize Japanese goods inspection teams. Resolution: Passed. (5) (6) (Omitted) (7) Ask the representatives attending the meeting to take an oath that they will never buy or sell Japanese goods. Resolution: The representatives attending the meeting took an oath on the spot. Those who did not attend will have the oath printed and distributed to all members and colleagues in the store to sign and seal, which must be completed within one week. The oath is recorded as follows: October 6, 20th year of the Republic of China, member representative of the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association, so-and-so, hereby solemnly swears that from this day on, I will never buy or sell Japanese goods, actively promote Chinese goods. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment from the industry. I swear.

Joint Meeting of the Medicinal Materials Industry: The Medicinal Materials Industry Association held a joint meeting with the industry group on the afternoon of the 6th. Thirty-two committee members attended. Chairman Xia Qizhen. (1) Inspection Team: It was resolved that from now on, 6 people will be appointed from 42 industry members every day, divided into two teams of three people each, responsible for inspection. The meal expenses of the inspectors will be borne by the industry group. If Japanese goods are found, a detailed report will be submitted to the association for review and handling. (2) Preparation for the Volunteer Army: The method will be handled in accordance with the instructions of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association.

The Coal Industry Association on the Purchase of Japanese Coal

Reported to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Coal Industry Association sent a letter yesterday stating: Greetings. I read the advertisement for coal bidding by the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau on the lower half of the fifth page of the second edition of the Shen Bao on October 7th. The full text is: "Our bureau's Wuting boiler requires approximately 250-260 tons of coal for winter heating. It must use 60% Fushun lump coal. Please open your prices and submit them to the General Affairs Department of our bureau at the Sichuan Road intersection. The bidding will be opened at the bureau on the afternoon of October 15th of the lunar calendar. We will place an order immediately. Special announcement." After investigation, Fushun lump coal is Japanese coal. At this time of national crisis, all our people have unanimously united to sever economic ties and strive to fulfill their duties. What is the intention of the director of the Telegraph Bureau, who dares to openly advertise to purchase Japanese coal? Is he not a traitor? The association believes that nothing less than a severe punishment can appease public anger. We hereby urgently send this letter and request your association to discuss and deal with it immediately to uphold justice.

As a result: (1) The association will organize a Japanese goods inspection team, and Wang Jianxun, Lu Zhankui, Yu Yongxiang, Gao Tailai, Yao Fusheng, Lu Hongji, and Lin Husheng were elected as Japanese goods inspectors. (2) How to reform the raw materials of the industry's Japanese goods will be handed over to the general assembly for handling. (3) The association will express its anti-Japanese stance by implementing a permanent economic severance and issuing a declaration. (4) The Huali Umbrella Factory's request to join the association will be answered after the Anti-Japanese Association reviews it. (5) It is reported that some members are still smuggling and selling Japanese goods. A letter should be sent to them to warn them and urge them to become aware. (6) The draft constitution of the association was revised and passed. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 p.m.

New Drug Industry Seals Japanese Medicines: The New Drug Industry Association sealed Japanese goods yesterday. National Salvation Ten-Person Group Held a Preparatory Meeting Yesterday: The Joint Association of the China National Salvation Ten-Person Group held a preparatory committee meeting on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Fellow Association the night before last. Xiong Shihui's Talk

Commander Xiong's arrival in Shanghai was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is heard that Xiong was very busy in Beijing. Because of the recent rumors in Shanghai, he made a special trip back to Shanghai. He originally planned to return to Beijing last night, but he received a telegram from the central government asking him to stay for a few more days, so he did not make the trip. Xiong went to the headquarters to work at 6:00 a.m. yesterday. It is heard that he will summon the staff for training tomorrow, fearing that the staff will neglect their duties because the central government ordered Chen Mingshu to concurrently serve as the Songhu Garrison Commander due to the Guangdong issue. Xiong spoke to reporters yesterday, and the records are as follows:

There have been many rumors in Shanghai in the past few days. Japanese residents and Chinese people in Zhabei have moved out one after another. Japanese residents are afraid of attacks by Chinese people, and Chinese people are afraid of attacks by Japanese troops. The mutual discord is entirely due to misunderstandings. The Chinese people's patriotic movement is law-abiding and will never take any action against ordinary Japanese residents. Therefore, Japanese residents can rest assured. The situation in Shanghai is different from that in Shenyang. Japan will not treat Shanghai the same way it treated Shenyang. However, some people deliberately spread rumors, such as what a certain Western newspaper reported today, saying that the Japanese consul had sent a letter to Mayor Zhang, saying that the Chinese government was unable to protect Japanese residents and that he would send troops to protect them himself. Mayor Zhang did not receive this letter. This is what I know. What the Western newspaper said is ridiculous. I believe that the Chinese local government in Shanghai has declared that it is responsible for protecting Japanese residents, and there will be no accidents. Several Japanese warships have arrived in Shanghai. In Japan, it is said that they came to reassure Japanese residents. However, this has aroused the resentment of the Chinese people. But if Japan wants to capture Songhu, they may not believe that the current military strength is sufficient. Therefore, there will be no accidents in Shanghai. This can be asserted.

Zhang Qun Went to Beijing Last Night

To Report the Situation in Shanghai to Chiang

Shanghai Mayor Zhang Qun took the express train to Beijing at 3:15 p.m. yesterday to report the security situation in Shanghai to Chairman Chiang. It is heard that Zhang will stay in Beijing for a day or two and then return to Shanghai.

Japanese Troops Deliberately Spread Panic

Chinese People Should Adopt Legitimate Defense

The Guowen News Agency reported that rumors suddenly arose in this port the day before yesterday (the 6th), causing students from various schools in Jiangwan to be excused from school by their parents. The atmosphere was very tense for a time, and residents in Zhabei were even more alarmed and moved to the concessions one after another. The rumors were especially rampant in the evening. However, it is heard that the rumors were actually caused by the Japanese navy setting up armed sentries in the areas outside the boundaries of the northwestern part of North Sichuan Road, causing panic among the citizens.

Page 10

Moreover, that area had already been recovered by our government. Although it was permissible to set up sentries to protect overseas Chinese in very tense times, there have been no incidents in this port recently that were unfavorable to Japanese overseas Chinese. Therefore, they were alarmed by the situation. In the evening, they secretly deployed Marine Corps soldiers in the vicinity, causing unrest among the Chinese. Yesterday, it was heard that the Public Security Bureau had reported to the Municipal Government to negotiate with them to avoid misunderstandings. However, by last night, the rumors seemed to have subsided slightly and were not as serious as the day before.

The Guangdong Middle and Elementary School Teachers and Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association sent a letter stating that in the past two days, it has been rumored that Japan is preparing to occupy the north and south of the two cities. The atmosphere is tense, and people are panicking. There are many people moving and relocating. Some say that this is a rumor and not worth worrying about. If so, it is certainly desirable. However, the Japanese are cunning and deceitful. How can we guarantee that they will not do anything? As evidenced by the Shenyang incident, they lined up to deploy defenses and set up electric nets, yet they declared that it was to prevent theft. We must give this kind of action deep consideration. Otherwise, once something happens suddenly, we will be at a loss and allow ourselves to be trampled on. The officials responsible for this port must also take this into account. Otherwise, the north and south of the two cities will be lost under the five words of calmness and non-resistance. I believe that defending the territory and governing the people, legitimate defense, is indispensable. Although weak countries have no justice, we absolutely cannot express our self-defense and be labeled as a standard of opposition. I believe that the civil and political parties in this port must quickly find a way to defend themselves. On the one hand, the government is responsible for announcing the self-defense policy to both Chinese and foreigners. If the Japanese have no indication of change, we can guarantee the safety of Japanese residents in the Chinese area. If the Japanese take any action, we vow to take legitimate defense. In this way, we will not be caught off guard and await death, nor will they take the opportunity to make excuses. May we all pay attention to this, which may not be a way to prevent trouble before it happens.

Ke Yinhang, Fei Xindun Requested the Japanese Consul

Pay Attention to the Security of the Concession

The Japanese Side Promised Not to Expand the Situation

However, Requesting Restrictions on the Anti-Japanese Movement

The recent dispatch of warships to Shanghai by Japan has caused panic among people from all walks of life. Although it is the result of self-disturbance by fools and the creation of rumors by a group of troublemakers, the various demonstrations by Japanese sailors in recent days, as well as the spreading of rumors by Japanese personnel, are indeed worthy of attention. This time, the Japanese warships came to Shanghai entirely at the arrogant request of the Japanese residents in Shanghai. Since the anti-Japanese patriotic movement in Shanghai, they have been racking their brains almost every day, holding secret meetings in the Japanese Club on Peng Road. The Shanghai Public Concession Bureau has long been paying attention to this. The day before yesterday, after the Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui came to Shanghai and discussed security matters with Mayor Zhang and others, the Director of the Concession Bureau, Fei Xindun, also convened Chinese and foreign directors to discuss this matter. As a result, Director Fei, after consulting with the leader of the consular body, the US Consul General Ke Yinhang, requested the Japanese consul to pay attention to the security of the entire Shanghai area and informed him that the lives and property of Japanese residents in the Chinese area were fully protected by the Chinese side, and the Concession Bureau was responsible for those in the concession. He advised the Japanese side not to disturb themselves in order to facilitate security. It is heard that the Japanese side has promised to do its best to restrain itself and will not expand the situation. However, it requested that the Concession authorities crack down on the anti-Japanese patriotic movement of the Chinese people, and also asked Ke and Fei to forward the request to our authorities to impose restrictions. Therefore, the security of Shanghai can be guaranteed to be completely worry-free.

Foreign Newspaper Reports

The Attitude of the Concession Bureau

Do Our Best to Maintain the Security of the Concession

Strictly Maintain Neutrality in the Sino-Japanese Dispute

The Da Mei Evening News stated that the Japanese newspapers in this port have criticized the Public Concession Bureau for not prohibiting the detention of Japanese goods. According to reliable sources, the criticism of the Japanese newspapers is unfounded. The Concession Bureau must strictly maintain neutrality in this Sino-Japanese dispute and cannot favor any side. The responsibility of the Concession Bureau is to protect the lives and property of residents in the concession, regardless of their nationality. The Concession Bureau is now doing its best to fulfill this responsibility. As for the detention of Japanese goods, nothing has been heard of it so far. Or there may be one or two unimportant and minor detention incidents. ○

But it must be known that the area of the concession is very large. The Concession Bureau cannot send patrols to guard every place where Japanese goods are sold or stored. At present, the hearts of Chinese and Japanese residents are extremely agitated. The Concession Bureau is strictly maintaining neutrality and maintaining law and order at all times.

Warships of Various Countries Stationed in Shanghai

The Great Powers Increase Their Naval Presence in Shanghai

Since Japan sent a squadron of twenty-four destroyers to Shanghai, the situation has become more tense than before. There are now seven Japanese warships in the Huangpu River, and the Ministry of the Navy will order the 9,885-ton special service ship Tokiwa to transport 400 members of the Yokosuka Naval Corps to Shanghai. The Tokiwa has four 200mm caliber guns and fourteen 150mm caliber guns. This ship is about to come to Shanghai. The United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Italy are paying close attention to the arrival of Japanese warships. The British and American East Asian Fleets have also increased their naval presence in Shanghai recently. The United States has dispatched another ship, the Heston, to Shanghai. There are currently fifteen foreign warships in the Huangpu River. The details are as follows:

In addition, there are a total of seven Japanese warships in the Huangpu River. In total, there are currently six British ships, five American ships, three French ships, and one Italian ship in Shanghai, plus Japan makes a total of twenty-two ships.

Tax Police Platoon Leader Suicide

Kang Baosen's Bitter Resentment of Violent Japan

A Far East News Agency report states that Kang Baosen, the third platoon leader of the first company of the second battalion of the Finance Ministry's tax police regiment, recently transferred from Bengbu to Shanghai, was a Liaoning native and a graduate of the Northeast Military Academy. Recently, due to the Japanese army's forcible occupation of the three northeastern provinces, he felt extreme indignation. Furthermore, considering that the authorities showed no sign of sending troops, he became even more agitated. Yesterday, at 1:30 PM, Platoon Leader Kang suddenly shot himself in the head with a pistol at the Longhua Garrison Headquarters. The bullet entered through the face and exited through the back of the head, causing profuse bleeding. The adjutant's office immediately sent someone to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment, where he was admitted to a second-class ward. He died from his severe injuries at around 4:00 PM. When the tragic news reached Longhua, officers and soldiers were deeply saddened. At the same time, Yang Zhengze, the second platoon leader of the same company, witnessed Kang's condition and was overcome with grief and indignation. The company commander, to prevent any untoward incidents, has dispatched personnel to keep watch.

National Day Reception for Foreign Guests

Yang Nianzu Notifies Separately

Yang Nianzu, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai, recently received instructions from the Ministry that on the occasion of the National Day celebration on the tenth of this month, the National Government would hold a celebration ceremony. In addition to notifying the ministers of various countries in Beijing and Ping, he was also instructed to notify the consulates of Japan, Italy, Norway, Czechoslovakia, Cuba, Turkey, Finland, Poland, and other countries in Shanghai to attend the ceremony in Beijing at that time. The number of accompanying persons should be indicated in advance to facilitate transportation arrangements. It is reported that Director Yang has already notified them separately upon receiving the order.

Guangxi Fellow Provincial Association's Telegram Advocates

Abandon Past Grievances

Save the Country Through Peace

Telegram to Beijing and Guangdong: To Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, Mr. Yu Youren, Mr. Hu Zhantang, and Mr. Dai Jitao in Nanjing; and Mr. Tang Shaochuan, Mr. Wang Jingwei, Mr. Sun Zhesheng, Mr. Zhang Puquan, Mr. Cai Yuanpei, Mr. Chen Bonan, Mr. Gu Xiangqin, and Mr. Li Delin in Guangzhou, Greetings. As national peril is imminent, it is fitting to unite against a common enemy. Internal strife among brothers should cease to resist foreign aggression. Since the loss of Liaoning and Jilin, the people's spirit has been greatly aroused, and the call for resistance against Japan has resounded throughout the country. It is incumbent upon you gentlemen, who have dedicated yourselves to the Party and the country, to lead the people and defend the nation. Now that the enemy troops are crossing the river, is it a time for leisurely discussion? You should quickly abandon past grievances, save the country through peace, respect public opinion, gather military resources, vigorously pursue revolutionary diplomacy, and recover lost territories within a specified time. It is imperative to prevent the violent Japanese from implementing their continental policy and to ensure the integrity of our country's territory and sovereignty. The millions of people of Guangxi pledge to follow the lead of the nation and spare no sacrifice to fight for the survival of the country and the nation. The situation is critical and urgent, and we can only hope for a swift resolution. The Guangxi Fellow Provincial Association in Shanghai for Anti-Japanese National Salvation, Yang.

Telegram to Guangxi: To Mr. Li Delin and Mr. Bai Jiansheng in Wuzhou; and to all division, brigade, and regimental commanders, government agencies, organizations, and newspapers, Greetings. The violent Japanese have seized our three provinces in Liaodong, creating unprecedented shame at home and abroad. The people of all regions have expressed their grief and fervent resolve, unanimously deciding to fight to the end and willing to be at the forefront. The brave men of Guangxi once advanced up the Xiang River to pacify the Central Plains and crossed the Yellow and Luo Rivers to secure the northern frontier. Their revolutionary achievements shine brightly throughout the universe. At this time of national crisis, it is especially important to inspire morale and jointly save the nation from danger. The people pay taxes to support the army, and the soldiers wield their weapons to defend the country. We are all Chinese, treading the same Chinese soil and doing the same Chinese work. Sacrificing homes and exhausting resources, our duty is beyond question. The Duke of Fan Wenzheng once said: "One should focus on the big picture and let go of the details, prioritize the urgent over the slow, and benefit the country without seeking personal gain." Please recite this to our armed comrades and elders of Guangxi. These are our sorrowful and indignant words, and we hope for your consideration. The Guangxi Fellow Provincial Association in Shanghai for Anti-Japanese National Salvation, Yang.

Prohibition of Unauthorized Rice Levies for Disaster Relief

Provincial Order for the Department of Civil Affairs to Investigate

The Shanghai Rice Grain Industry Trade Association received a reply from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce stating: "In response to your letter of September 28, which forwarded a telegram from the Wuxi Rice Grain Shipping Industry Association stating that the Liyang County Government had improperly acceded to the request of the disaster relief branch to levy rice donations, which hindered the people's food supply, and requested a transfer to cancel it, we immediately telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering a strict investigation and prohibition. Now, we have received a substitute telegram No. 1334, which reads: 'The substitute telegram has been noted. The county magistrate's unauthorized levy of rice donations without prior approval is indeed inappropriate. In addition to ordering the Department of Civil Affairs to investigate and report for review, you are hereby notified accordingly.' Therefore, we have recorded the telegram and hope that you will investigate and notify accordingly."

News of Disaster Relief Efforts

Chinese and Foreign Relief Association's Disaster Relief Work

New and Old Cotton Clothes Shipped Out: The Chinese and Foreign Relief Association shipped out a large quantity of relief clothing yesterday. In addition to distributing all the old clothes donated by philanthropists, the first batch of new cotton clothes made by the Association has also been completed and shipped out at the same time. This includes (Xinghua) four packages of old clothes, 960 pieces, 25 packages of new cotton clothes, 1,000 pieces; (Yancheng) four packages of old clothes, 1,320 pieces, 25 packages of new cotton clothes, 1,000 pieces; (Dongtai) five packages of old clothes, 1,800 pieces, 25 packages of new cotton clothes, 1,000 pieces; (Taizhou) 25 packages of new cotton clothes, 1,000 pieces. All of the above were shipped out yesterday, along with one box of medicated oil for each location. Also, (Yangzhou) 25 packages of new cotton clothes, totaling 1,000 pieces, and one box of medicated oil, will be shipped out today.

Overseas Chinese Continue to Send Large Sums: The Association received the following disaster relief donations from overseas Chinese yesterday: (1) Saigon Overseas Chinese China Flood Relief Association, 40,000 taels of silver; (2) Saigon Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, 35,000 taels of silver; (3) Honolulu Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, sixth remittance of 10,000 US dollars; (4) San Francisco Chinese Consolidated Benevolent Association, second remittance of 10,000 US dollars.

Painter Lian Run Helps with Relief: Painters Chen Dieye and Qian Shoutie sent a letter to the Association the other day, proposing to collaborate on 100 Buddhist images, each selling for 30 yuan, regardless of size, but those requiring inscriptions will be doubled in price. The Chinese and Foreign Relief Association will collect the pieces, and all the proceeds will be used for disaster relief. Since it is possible to obtain the masterpieces of famous artists and save the disaster victims, it is believed that elegant and charitable people will be happy to order them.

Overseas Chinese in Burma Raise White Rice for Disaster Relief

This time, various provinces in our country have been hit by floods, and wails of despair are heard everywhere. Overseas Chinese abroad are deeply concerned and look inward. Places such as the Philippines, Singapore, Java, and Siam are all enthusiastically donating and raising funds to be remitted here. Recently, the Overseas Chinese Business Association in Burma raised 2,500 bags of white rice, and the Yangon Sideris Rice Company raised 1,500 bags of white rice, estimated to be worth about 43,000 taels of silver. Yesterday, it was transported to Shanghai by the Dirahwa liner. This righteous grain and benevolent act is deeply admirable. In addition to the National Government's Flood Relief Committee designating 2,000 bags for Yuezhou and 2,000 bags for Funing to be distributed in the disaster areas to help the people's food supply and issuing official receipts directly to the above-mentioned two groups and publishing thank-you notices in the newspapers, the enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese in raising relief funds and their righteous reputation spreading far and wide is truly admirable.

News from the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association

Implementation Plan for Guaranteeing Cattle Loans and Seeds: The Association, together with the Jiangsu Provincial Disaster Relief Committee, the Jiangsu Flood Emergency Relief Association, and the Jiangbei Flood Temporary Relief Association, held a joint meeting on the 1st of this month. Commissioner He Yushu proposed that the relief agencies assist the Department of Agriculture in handling cattle loan and seed matters. It was resolved that the Department of Agriculture would directly consult with the two relief associations to handle the matter. It is reported that the Association had previously sent letters to the county offices and bureaus, asking them to consult with local officials and gentry on the matter of protecting livestock and provide appropriate subsidies based on their remaining resources, depending on the severity of the disaster in each county. The matter of providing seed loans is also being planned.

The Fourth District of Dongtai Begs for Relief and Appeals: The Association recently received a plea for relief from the Disaster Relief Committee of the Fourth District of Dongtai, which has been stricken by floods. The original text is extracted below: "The Fourth District is located downstream of the three counties of Tai, Dong, and Xing, with a low-lying terrain, serving as the final outlet for western waters into the sea. This summer's torrential rains have caused a disaster, with all three dams releasing water simultaneously, resulting in floods flowing horizontally, turning the entire Fourth District into a marsh. Furthermore, the dikes and sluices of the Yancheng Reclamation Company blocked the waterways, preventing drainage, causing water accumulation in the district, with a source but no outlet, causing great harm. Since the breaches of the You and Shao dams, the water surged down, and the water level in the Fourth District suddenly increased by several feet, coupled with strong winds and rapid currents, causing the surrounding dikes in various villages to collapse one after another, without exception. The vast expanse of water submerged the entire territory. The autumn grains, which were about to be harvested, were completely submerged, and the houses were also washed away. Cries of despair echoed through the fields, with no way to seek help. The most tragic were the elderly and weak, who had no time to escape, and countless people died. The young and strong were either , or , with no food during the day and no light at night, sleeping in the wind, awaiting death helplessly. Corpses floated, and livestock wandered, making the scene unbearable to witness. This catastrophic disaster is unprecedented. Although the colleagues of our Association have rushed to various villages by boat to do their best to rescue and resettle some people, or send them out of the affected area, the disaster is too large, and rescue cannot keep up. The future is long, and it is difficult to maintain. The Fourth District is located on the coast and is known for its poverty, coupled with frequent famines. At this time, raising relief donations is extremely difficult. Even if there are a few donations, they are like a drop in the bucket, unable to help in the slightest. Looking at the ocean and sighing, we can only cry in vain. But remembering the tens of thousands of dying disaster victims, groaning in the midst of the great flood, emaciated and waiting to be fed, if we do not urgently seek proper solutions, they will surely fill the ditches. We, the colleagues, witness this and feel heartbroken. Therefore, we make this appeal on their behalf, earnestly requesting charitable organizations and generous philanthropists to have compassion for those who are hungry and drowning, and to work together to achieve effective results. Whether it is dry food, the more the better, or relief donations, may they come continuously. May your kindness spread far and wide, and may you provide support and assistance. Then the disaster victims will be grateful and remember your kindness forever. Our Association respectfully bows nine times on behalf of the disaster victims."

Eurasia Aviation Corporation

Northwest Line Trial Flight Period

The Areas Flown Over Are Still Peaceful

Gasoline Must Be Transferred from Ping

Trial Flight Possible in Mid-Next Month

Mr. Li Jingcong's Talk

A reporter from the Daily News visited Mr. Li Jingcong, Director of the Operations Group of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, yesterday. According to him, the company's new Northwest route has been in preparation for a long time. The route flies through Zhengzhou, Shanzhou, Xi'an, Pingliang, Lanzhou, Liangzhou, Ganzhou, Suzhou, Anxi, Hami, and Urumqi, directly to the endpoint of Yining in Xinjiang. The company is sponsored by the Ministry of Communications. Matters such as the transportation situation in each area, whether there are motor roads and other roads, whether the locality is peaceful, whether there is a flat ground of 300 meters in length and width, whether there are obstacles around the flat ground, and whether gasoline for aircraft use can be purchased locally are of great importance to flight. The company has telegraphed the governments of the four provinces of Yu, Shan, Gan, and Xin to request a detailed investigation. Now, it is reported that the provinces of Yu and Shan have replied to the Ministry. Mr. Li saw the reply telegram in Beijing, which stated that the area was generally peaceful, but gasoline could not be purchased. This telegram has not yet been formally transferred to the company. As for the provinces of Xin and Gan, due to inconvenient transportation, mail and telegrams are sent slowly, and it is not yet known whether the Ministry's telegram has been received. Recently, the company has been actively preparing for a trial flight and has decided to purchase gasoline and transfer it from Beiping to GuiSui and other places for use. The gasoline is expected to arrive in various places at the beginning of next month at the earliest, and a new type of aircraft can be dispatched for the first trial flight in mid-month. After the trial flight is successful, business will begin. At that time, the provincial governments can transfer orders to military and political organs to protect the route along the way.

Customs Cracks Down on the Transport of Silver Small Coins

Ministry of Finance Promulgates Seven Measures for Circulation

In order to safeguard the currency policy and facilitate merchants and the people, the Ministry of Finance has synthesized past cases and taken into account the current situation to formulate seven measures to crack down on the transportation of silver small coins, so as to unify the policy and facilitate implementation. All previous orders issued by the old Ministry of Finance in Beiping and the former Currency Bureau prohibiting transportation should be uniformly canceled, effective from the first day of this month. The Jianghai Customs has received this Ministry order and has implemented it since the first day of this month. The measures are recorded below: (1) Whenever inferior and lightweight small coins privately cast for profit-making purposes are found at various checkpoints, they shall be handled in accordance with these measures. (2) Before the implementation of the Currency Law, single silver small coins with a total weight of 7.2 li in Kuping (Treasury Standard), equivalent to 0.504 mace of pure silver, and double silver small coins with a total weight of 1.44 qian, equivalent to 1.08 mace of pure silver, shall be temporarily allowed to circulate according to local customs. (3) Regardless of whether single or double silver small coins do not meet the weight and fineness of the previous item, they shall be considered inferior and lightweight coins. (4) All inferior and lightweight coins found shall be melted into silver. After deducting transportation and melting expenses, 20% shall be turned over to the government, and 20% of the government funds shall be used for awards. The remaining silver shall be returned to the original transporter for collection. (5) All non-inferior and lightweight coins, whether single or double, in amounts less than 500 coins, shall be allowed for merchants to transport freely, and shall be released after inspection by various Jianghai Customs. If the amount exceeds 500 coins, a passport must be obtained from the Customs Superintendency of the place of shipment before they can be transported. (6) When issuing passports, the Customs Superintendency of each customs shall first ascertain the reported quantity, type, and destination of the goods, and clearly state them in the passport. (7) If the Customs finds silver small coins transported without a passport or in excess of the amount specified in the passport, except for inferior and lightweight coins, which shall be melted and handed over to the government according to the above item, if they are non-inferior and lightweight coins, 3% shall be used for awards, and the remainder shall be returned.

Meal Expenses Transferred to Patriotic Donations

Initiated by Employees of the Yingchang Factory

Other Factories and Stores Can Emulate

The entire staff of the Shanghai Yingchang Factory of the Great China Match Company in Pudong, in view of the ongoing national crisis, specifically resolved the other day to suspend the meal for the Double Tenth Festival and deposit all meal expenses of more than 100 yuan into the Pudong Bank for future use as patriotic donations.

Self-Built Five-Story Building

Has Already Started Business

The Shanghai Silk Industry Commercial Savings Bank, organized by the tycoons of the silk industry and the financial sector in this city, has been formally established.
