Opening of He Hing Wharf and Warehouse Company

Mr. Yue Zhenbao, Mr. Lu Bohong, Mr. Zhang Xiaoliang, Mr. Wang Yunfu, and Mr. Yu Baoqing, all Shanghai gentlemen, in view of the development of shipping since the recovery of our country's autonomy, which has progressed rapidly, and the fact that the original wharves in this port were all old-fashioned and insufficient to meet current needs, raised funds to purchase more than 80 mu of land in Zhoujiadu, Pudong, to build three steel floating wharves and a state-of-the-art three-story steel-concrete warehouse, which can store 200,000 packages of groceries. The terrain is higher than Puxi (Pudong), and the water depth is very deep, with a water depth of more than 20 feet even at the lowest tide. Large and small ships can be berthed at any time. The drawings were planned by Mr. Gu Daosheng of the Gongli Business Company, making it the most complete wharf and warehouse in this port. It opened yesterday. The company provided a special boat to transport guests, and more than a thousand people from all walks of life successively went to visit. They were warmly received by the managers and guided to see various departments, all of whom expressed satisfaction. Tea and snacks were also provided, and everyone dispersed happily.

Baoyu Lane Rent Increase Concession

After the Dehe Foreign Firm, the landlord of Baoyu Lane on Route Edward VII in the French Concession, announced that the rent would be increased by 30% across the board from November 1, the tenants were panicked and organized a Tenants' Union to send a letter to the Dehe Foreign Firm requesting that the order to increase rent be withdrawn. It has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper that the Dehe Foreign Firm has inquired about the tenants' request and reduced the rent increase for houses along the road by 10%, and for residents in the lane by half. Mr. Chen was dispatched by the firm to reply orally. However, the tenants of the lane believe that the commercial situation is grim and the market is panicking to the extreme. The cost of rice is as precious as pearls, and firewood is as expensive as cinnamon. The rent that the tenants usually bear is already barely enough to make ends meet. They want to follow in the footsteps of Zhizhong, Shixian, Yuqing and other lanes in this concession and demand a rent reduction (Zhizhong and other lanes have already implemented rent reductions), how can they bear any more burden? The tenants are now preparing to send a letter to the Dehe Foreign Firm again, making a second request, in order to cancel the rent increase proposal and to help merchants in difficulty.

Male Corpse on the Riverside in Lujiazui

Sixteen-Character Last Words

Bad Environment, Economic Oppression

Taking This Approach, There Is No Other Reason

The No. 2 patrol boat of the Tongren Fuyuantang Rescue Bureau found a male drowning corpse on the riverside in Lujiazui, Pudong, at around 1:00 PM yesterday. The corpse was about 30 years old. After the corpse was recovered, it was observed that the corpse was wearing a gray striped Serge long gown, a black floral satin padded jacket, gray crepe gauze padded pants, a white flannel short shirt, red willow-patterned foreign cloth single pants, a white Xiangyun waistband, purple thread socks, and navy blue serge shoes, with gray silk ribbons to tie the feet. Two cards were found beside him, one for Qian Fengyi, barrister at Law, Fessenden Road, No. 3 Xinkang Lane, Jiangxi Road, and one with the words Yan Diling, Xi Jiu, Guangrao, etc. There was also a 10% off coupon from the Kuaihuo Lin Food Company for the Bingyin year, and a piece of paper with the words "Bad environment, economic oppression, taking this approach, there is no other reason" written in blue ink. It was then known that the man had committed suicide by throwing himself into the river. He was immediately taken back to the bureau in Nanmatou for coffining and recognition according to regulations.

The Massive Sandalwood Theft Case at the Okura Warehouse

A major theft occurred at the Okura warehouse in Pudong last month. The stolen items were twenty pieces of sandalwood, imported from India and stored at the warehouse, of considerable value. Upon discovering the theft, it was found that the doors and windows around the warehouse were untouched. It remains unknown how such large cargo was moved in and out. The warehouse immediately issued a loss report and reported it to the First Sub-Bureau of the Third District, requesting assistance in tracking down the stolen goods. The sub-bureau then reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which issued a general order to all district offices to investigate. On the 2nd of this month, detectives from the Water Patrol Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau discovered that the stolen goods had been purchased by the Yi Cheng Ning Cargo Company at the Zhuhang Wharf in the Southern City. Zhu Haifan, the owner of the company, found it inconvenient to store such a large quantity of goods in his company, so he transported them to the Fengtai Grain Store, opened by his elder brother Zhu Haishan near Sanguantang on Zhaojia Road in the Western Gate, for storage and gradual sale. The detectives immediately went to the address, detained Zhu Haifan, and then went to the Fengtai store, where they apprehended Zhu Haishan and a store employee named Wu Zhumei. Knowing that the matter was exposed, Zhu Haishan handed over four burlap sacks of sandalwood, but these were not the original stolen goods, but rather an attempt to cover up the crime. The detectives brought the suspects to the team, where after preliminary interrogation by Chief Xu, they were transferred to the First Sub-Bureau of the Third District in Pudong for interrogation. On the previous day, detectives from the same team learned that a batch of stolen goods from the case had been sold by the Zhu Haifan and Zhu Haishan brothers to the Yuan Yu Yong Hardware and Sundries Store on Limadu Road in the Southern City. They immediately reported this information to the team leader, who immediately dispatched Inspector Li Wenmo to go to the Yuan Yu Yong store with the Chief of the First District General Office to inquire with the store manager, Pu Ruihe, whether the store had purchased sandalwood. Pu claimed that the store had been established for many years and had a solid reputation, and would never buy goods of unknown origin. Inspector Li and others did not pursue the matter. Before long, they suddenly discovered two burlap sacks of the original stolen sandalwood, totaling fourteen large pieces (each piece worth over one hundred yuan), among the piles of sundry goods in the store. They immediately seized the goods and questioned Pu. Pu's face turned pale, and he remained silent. They detained Pu and took him and the recovered stolen goods back to the team. During the preliminary hearing, Pu confessed that he was forty years old and from Wuxi. He claimed that the sandalwood was acquired through a broker named Shao Fulin and that Yi Cheng Company had issued an invoice. He insisted that he was momentarily confused, leading him to receive the stolen goods. Considering the severity of the theft, they were instructed to prepare a written report and transfer the suspect and stolen goods to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Bestiality Case: Imprisonment for Three Years and Six Months

Mao Xingfu, a 20-year-old man from Jiangbei, broke into the Gongda Yarn Factory workshop at 252 Huasheng Road around 8 PM on the 29th of last month. He forcibly raped Sun Lanying, an 18-year-old woman from Taixing. In the early hours, the woman's cousin, Ji Ruicheng, confronted Mao, leading to a fight. Chinese detectives Zhang Yunjian and Liu Changgen from the Yangshupu Police Station arrested both Mao and Ji and handed them over to the First Special District Court for interrogation. The details have been previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xie-fen presided over the Third Criminal Court, sentencing Mao Xingfu to three years and six months of imprisonment. The number of days spent in detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Ji Ruicheng was fined five yuan with a two-year suspended sentence.

Arrest of Suspects in the Murder of Hart

Planning Another Robbery in Pudong

Awaiting Transfer by the Municipal Public Security Bureau

On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month at 5 PM, Detective Li Xiaobao of the Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested Zhang Zhangsheng, a thief from Pudong, on Zhongshan Road. A loaded handgun was found on him. He confessed that his accomplice, Yao Jinxiang, from Jiangbei, was hiding at No. 111 Taopeng Road, Yangshupu. The day before yesterday, Li asked the Yangshupu Police Station for assistance in arresting him. The police chief dispatched Chinese detective Liu Changsheng and Western detective Hyde to secretly arrest him. They found nothing. Later, Yao was arrested at the First Floor Teahouse at No. 675 on the same road. Li Zhang, a woman from Pudong (Zhang Chengsheng's sister), was also taken into the police station for separate detention. Yesterday morning, they were handed over to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police station, stated that Yao Jinxiang and Zhang Zhangsheng were involved in the murder of a Westerner named Hart (an employee of the Whangpoo Conservancy Board) on the Bund on May 30th of last year. When Zhang Zhangsheng was arrested, he and Yao Jinxiang were planning to rob somewhere in Pudong. Zhang Zhangsheng also confessed at the police station that the handgun had been hidden at his sister Li Zhang's place in the past, and that she had instructed him to go to Pudong for robbery that day. Subsequently, the Chinese and Western detectives reported the circumstances of the arrest of the two defendants. Detective Ji Xiaobao of the Municipal Public Security Bureau recounted the circumstances of Zhang's arrest. Zhang Zhangsheng testified that he was not involved in the case of killing the Westerner. The handgun was given to him by Zhang Along, who was on the run, to be stored at his sister Li Zhang's place. His remaining statements were evasive. Yao Jinxiang confessed that he had borrowed money from Zhang Zhangsheng before, but he was not involved in theft. Li Zhang confessed that her brother Zhang Zhangsheng asked her to borrow money but she did not have it, so she falsely claimed that someone wanted to buy a handgun and that he could sell it to get money. She tricked him to go halfway where he was arrested by detectives from the Public Security Bureau. She denied any involvement in the planned robbery in Pudong, and asked for leniency. Judge Xiao Xie-fen verified the confessions and ordered them to be detained separately, awaiting the Municipal Public Security Bureau to prepare a document and transfer them back to the case for further investigation.

Huang Chunquan Accuses Chen Laowu of Three Crimes

Huang Chunquan, a native of Shaoxing who works in the paper industry and currently resides above the Shengli Copper Bed Store at Hongxingli on Beijing Road, filed a complaint because he was impoverished, had many children, and could not make a living. Li Xialing Commits Suicide in a Hotel

Around 3 PM the day before yesterday, a man named Li Xialing, 21 years old, went alone to the Huayang Hotel on Sima Road and booked room number 30 to stay. Beautiful Young Woman on the Shuntian Steamer

Suspected Trafficker's Contradictory Statements Lead to Arrest

Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang, investigators from the Relief Association, and Wu Rongsheng, a detective from the Water Patrol, boarded the Shuntian steamer yesterday and found a young woman who was very beautiful and fashionably dressed. Because she was a lone female passenger with no luggage, they questioned her. She claimed her name was Zhou Peifen, from Nanxiang, and that her husband, Wang Xingsheng, worked as a partner in the Daoxiangcun in Tianjin and had been gone for many years. While they were questioning her, a man from Tianjin named Yan Guizhen came over and claimed that she was the wife of his friend and that he had sent her on the ship. He asked them not to question her. The investigators asked him where her husband was, and he claimed that he was shopping ashore. When asked the name of the woman's husband, he suddenly stared blankly and did not answer, his statements contradictory. They wanted to arrest him, but he had already escaped. They identified him as a trafficker and arrested the woman as well and took them both to the police station for interrogation.

Four Arrested and Handed Over to the Court

Yuan Zhaoxiang, residing at No. 4 Yongqingli, Caojiadu, Shanghai West, possessed some wealth and was considered a family of modest means. He suddenly received a threatening letter demanding three thousand yuan. Yuan ignored it. Unexpectedly, he received four more threatening letters in succession, and they even arranged to meet near the cemetery, with the money to be placed next to a black coffin. Yuan immediately handed over the original letter to the Sixth District Police Station, asking for protection. Unexpectedly, at night, four people suddenly arrived with flashlights and shone them on the black coffin. The detectives rushed up and arrested all four bandits, escorting them to the station. They confessed to being Cao Azhong, Chen Sanyuan, Zhou Dongyang, and Huang Decai. They were immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau and handed over to the local court for interrogation yesterday.

Unauthorized Use of a Truck Causes an Accident

Three Children and One Man Injured

Yesterday afternoon around 5 PM, Wang Guisheng, the owner of the Wang Shengji Truck Company on Jessfield Road, Shanghai West, drove his truck, No. 3794, to Fanhangdu to visit friends. He parked the truck on the side of the road opposite the lumberyard. Unexpectedly, after Wang got out of the truck, his relative Xu Rongsheng, only 17 years old, got into the truck and, playing around, turned on the engine. The truck drove straight forward and onto the sidewalk. Fortunately, someone nearby jumped on and applied the brakes, but it had already hit three children and one man who were sitting and standing in front of the door, all of whom were injured and fell to the ground. Several wooden benches and sundry items were also damaged. A patrol officer saw this and stepped forward, arresting them all and bringing them back to the Sixth District Police Station. The injured parties were identified as Ye Along, 6 years old; Huang Amei, 6 years old; Wang Jincai, 6 years old; and Wang Ashun, 29 years old, all local residents. The police immediately dispatched a police car to take them to the hospital for diagnosis and treatment. They then prepared a written report and handed over the perpetrator, Xu Rongsheng, to the local court for interrogation.

The American aviator Charles Lindbergh and his wife are scheduled to return home today for a funeral. Chen Shaokuan Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Chen Shaokuan, Director of the Naval Academy and concurrently Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning. According to what Chen told a reporter from the Guowen News Agency, Minister Yang has not yet set a date to go to Nanjing due to the extended Fourth Plenary Session. In this port area, due to various rumors from the outside, the defenses are stricter than usual. Currently moored in the port are seven or eight ships, including the Yong Sui, Chu Tai, Yong Jian, Chen Zi, Ding An, and Hua An. Each port along the Yangtze River has these ships. The people's morale is indeed high, but it can be maintained by remaining calm. As long as the central government negotiates, there is no fear of not achieving victory. There is indeed hope for peace in Guangzhou, but the matter is being handled by the central government, so the details are not known. After arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, Chen went to the aircraft station and various ships under construction for inspection. It is said that due to urgent ministerial affairs, he will return to Nanjing that night. The rumors circulating outside the night before last that the Japanese navy was plotting to occupy Gaochangmiao were unfounded, as everything was peaceful as usual yesterday.

Called by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Record of the National Products Manufacturers' Congress

Letter Sent to Five National Products Associations

Great Cooperative Organization

Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened the All-Shanghai National Products Manufacturers' Congress. Attendees included over a hundred companies, such as Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company, Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory, China Apple Factory, Hua Mao Cap Store, Wuzhou Soap Factory, China Chemical Industrial Society, Sanyou Industrial Society, Samsung Cotton Iron Factory, Da Zhonghua Match Factory, and others, with several hundred representatives in total, making it a grand occasion. Chairman Wang Wanju presided over the meeting, Zhong Jinzhen recorded the minutes, and the ceremony proceeded as usual. First, Chairman Wang stated, "Today, our chamber convened the All-Shanghai National Products Manufacturers' Congress. I am very honored to have all of you present. I, in my capacity as Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, will briefly present the reasons for convening this meeting to all the representatives. Our chamber, in view of Japan taking advantage of our natural disasters and banditry to brazenly send troops, occupy Yuaning, seize the East Railway, kill our people, and plunder our wealth, and not satisfied with even that, dispatching warships to spy on fortresses in various provinces and landing to demonstrate, their ambition and brutality is causing global outrage. Our people feel the pain firsthand. When the bad news came, everyone was shocked and sought ways to restrain themselves and devise plans for retaliation. Our national products merchants, whose duty is to promote national products to stem the leakage of wealth, have a great relationship with this national crisis. This is the purpose of today's congress. Recently, various newspapers have revealed detailed information about Japan's actions and the diplomatic situation, and public opinion is boiling. I believe all the representatives are already aware of this. But if we investigate the reason, Japan has an excessive population and increasing unemployment. Furthermore, in recent years, our country's citizens have gradually awakened. They anticipate that in a few years, our country's national products will sell well, and Japanese trade in China will inevitably plummet. Therefore, they use a preemptive strategy to wantonly destroy. Their premeditation is not a matter of a day or two. After this incident, fortunately, our people united in their efforts and expressed thorough and painful sentiments. For example, at the previous All-Shanghai Citizens' Congress, the number of attendees reached over 100,000, an unprecedented number in Shanghai. If we can consistently implement this unity to the end, it will be enough to make the Japanese feel cold. We merchants can only adhere to the principle of 'speaking commerce from a commercial standpoint' and think from the perspective of merchants. Although our country's commerce has made some progress in recent years, it is simply impossible to compare with Japan, the United States, and other countries. We, who are responsible for promoting national products, from now on, should strive to improve the manufacturing of goods, the sourcing of raw materials, the selection of quality, the research on decoration, the assessment of prices, and the convenience of use. We must firmly adhere to the principle of truthfulness and not have such malpractices as mixing inferior goods with superior ones or selling inferior goods at high prices, which would lead to the loss of morality and the decline of credibility, and become an obstacle to the future of national products. This is what our chamber hopes for, first. Our country's national products have been greatly affected by the invasion of foreign goods. The majority of the people are happy to use foreign goods and reject national products. The reason for this is not that our people lack patriotism, but that foreign goods are cheap and of good quality, which deeply meets the psychology of Chinese people, especially women. In other words, the credibility of our country's national products has been lost for a long time. In reality, they are not as good as foreign goods in many ways, and transportation and agricultural industries are also not advanced, so the result is always unable to resist the influx and sales of foreign goods. The representatives are all enthusiastic, patriotic, honest, and upright merchants. From now on, you should think from this perspective and pay more attention to try to reverse this decline. This is what our chamber hopes for, second. Shanghai is the best in our country's industrial and commercial achievements. In this situation of resisting goods, our Shanghai has a significant role. From now on, how should we strive to unite, have a long-term vision, hold a fearless spirit, and persevere to the end, without being a five-minute heat, and giving people cause for mockery? This is what our chamber hopes for, third. Our chamber's national products market has always aimed to promote national products and develop domestic and foreign trade, collecting excellent national products and selling them at reasonable prices, so people come to purchase them in an endless stream, and it can be called the hub of the national products industry. At this time of national crisis, we plan to adopt the opinions of the national products industry, expand publicity, and give the knowledge of national products to all the Shanghai and Chinese compatriots, so that everyone can agree that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's national products market is the only large market that promotes national products and sells them at reasonable prices, directly boosting the sales of national products and indirectly restraining the Japanese. The representatives are not lacking in capable people. I hope they will express their opinions as much as possible to serve as a guiding needle. This is what our chamber hopes for, fourth. Our chamber has convened this congress with these four points in mind, in order to plan with you all, hoping that we can proceed in unison, without slackening or neglecting. Our chamber would be fortunate, and China would be fortunate. Then, Mr. Zhang Zilian, representative of the Samsung Factory, Mr. Ji Jiannan, representative of the Sanyou Society, Mr. Xiang Kangyuan, representative of the Kangyuan Factory, Mr. Zhou Hekang, representative of the Universal Factory, and others gave speeches, expressing extremely painful sentiments. The words were long but concise. It was decided on the spot to organize the Shanghai National Products Factories Anti-Japanese National Salvation Congress, initiate the formation of volunteer armies to be the government's support, and ask the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to notify the trade associations to relay the matter to each manufacturer for responsible handling, and to submit a proposal requesting the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send a letter to the five national products associations to seek opinions and unite into one large national products organization, so that they can concentrate their strength and unite. The meeting adjourned around 7 PM.

The Shanghai Municipal Council

Increase in Police Rate Next Year

Restoring the Old Rate of Sixteen Percent

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Council announced that it plans to increase the police rate next year, restoring the old rate of sixteen percent. In recent years, the world economy has been depressed, and all regions have felt financial constraints. The Municipal Council could hardly avoid being affected. According to the report submitted by the Accounting Department to the Board of Directors, the Council's finances have been greatly affected by the continued shrinkage of exchange rates. Combined with other reasons, it is expected that by the end of this fiscal year, not only will the surplus of 300,000 taels originally listed in the budget be exhausted, but there will also be a large deficit. It is found that within the current year's operating budget, the surplus of 2,271,568 taels from last year was used to offset the deficit. Therefore, if the next year's budget cannot increase income, then even if expenditures are maintained at this year's level, there will still be a deficit of at least 2,900,000 taels. Therefore, the Accounting Department proposed that, on the one hand, the heads of each department should carefully study the department's expenditures and consult with the Accounting Department to find effective ways to reduce government spending. On the other hand, the taxpayers should be informed in advance of the necessity to restore the old police rate next year. In addition, it is also planned to re-evaluate land prices next year and levy taxes according to the evaluation in 1933. These proposals have now been approved by the Board of Directors. The Council has already rigorously implemented frugality in expenditures. Even if it makes every effort to reduce government spending next year, it will still not be enough to make up for the deficit. It will inevitably have to restore the sixteen percent rate. The Accounting Department had already anticipated this matter in March of this year at the Finance Committee and in April at the Western Taxpayers' Annual Budget Meeting. Therefore, it was said at the time that if the exchange rate could not greatly increase in the short term, it would be necessary to restore the donation rate before July 1930 in 1932. Now everyone knows that the silver price has fallen to a new low, and it has only rebounded in recent weeks. The Shanghai Municipal Council's donation

Page 12

rate is also unnecessarily repeated. If it were not for the sale of the Electricity Department, it would probably have increased to 20 percent now, which would be difficult to control as it is now. As for the Electricity Department's sale price of 81 million taels, it will be paid off in five years. Of which 54 million taels will be used to redeem the Municipal Council's public bonds. The remaining 27 million taels was originally designated for capital expenditures. Only the interest payable by the Shanghai Electric Power Company on the unpaid sale price is allocated to the operating expenses. In the future, the Accounting Department also plans to change the original policy and store approximately 12 million taels of the estimated allocations for capital expenditures in the 1932 and 1933 sales for temporary emergency expenditures and to offset the deficit in operating expenses in the next few years. As for the original construction program, it will need to be slightly delayed, and the required funds are planned to be raised using the prevailing method of issuing bonds.

Chinese Ships Transporting Japanese Rice

Armed Protection During Loading

The Japanese military's occupation of our country's territory has aroused the common hatred of all our people. The business community's economic disengagement is proceeding particularly severely. The exchange of Japanese goods has been greatly reduced. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, a large batch of Japanese rice at the dock of the Osaka Company, a Japanese company in Yangshupu in this port, needed to be loaded for various ports such as Nanjing. A certain shipping company in Shanghai dispatched two of its ships to the dock for packaging, one ship for loading first, and the other for continued transport. With the prior consent of the Japanese company, Japanese people carrying handguns and weapons were stationed around the dock to guard the rice being loaded onto the ship. Small fireboats were also dispatched in the Huangpu River to provide armed protection. The first ship was fully loaded last night and is scheduled to leave Shanghai this morning.

County Affiliates Busily Handling the Rush漕 [Grain Transport] and Accepting Bundling Businesses

The Shanghai County's bundling business system has been restored by the county bureau's clear order to facilitate the rush grain transport and collection. It is now known that the district chiefs are now gathering the township chiefs and bundling business representatives to discuss the turnover. All matters will be completed before the 15th of this month. This year's winter grain transport collection will be handled by the bundling businesses. All of this year's busy money and old debts will still be the responsibility of the township chiefs to collect and close the accounts.

Provincial Order Reiterating the Prohibition of Rice Exports

The Shanghai County Government received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, "It is found that rice and grain in Jiangsu Province have always been prohibited from being privately transported out of the province, and orders have been repeatedly issued to strictly prohibit this. This year, various counties have suffered from continuous rain, resulting in a poor autumn harvest. Regarding the private transport of rice and grain out of the province, the prohibition should be reiterated to maintain the people's food supply. It is hereby ordered that the county magistrate order a thorough investigation. If there are any cases of transporting rice out of the province or leaking to the sea, they should be investigated and dealt with. Rice should continue to circulate normally among the counties within this province, and prices should not be suppressed under any pretext. There should be no delays or violations." This order.

Changes in the Pacific Institute

Decision to be Made at the Meeting on the 12th

The Pacific International Institute had previously decided to hold a meeting in Hangzhou on the 21st of this month. However, recently, due to the issue of the Japanese representatives' attendance, changes have occurred. Therefore, the previously decided date of the 21st for the meeting may not be realized. However, according to Mr. Green, chairman of the administrative council of the institute, as told to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, the meeting will likely be decided by the board of directors at the affairs meeting on the 12th or 13th. Here is a record of the conversation between Xu Xinliu and Chen Liting, our agents-general.

Xu-Chen Conversation: Each member country of the institute has a director or honorary agent-general. The agent-general of our country is Mr. Yu Rizhang. Mr. Yu has recently been ill and replaced by Mr. Xu Xinliu as agent. According to what he told a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, regarding the previous report that the Japanese representatives would not attend the formal meeting, this is the opinion of some foreign representatives. However, this matter cannot be raised to Japan, not only by our representatives but also by other foreign representatives. It can only be said that the Japanese representatives themselves have expressed their intention not to attend. Therefore, whether this meeting will be held as scheduled will depend on the decision of the board of directors of each country at the meeting on the 12th. According to representative Chen Liting, the Japanese representatives believe that it is unsafe to hold the meeting in Hangzhou and do not intend to participate. However, they believe that a meeting without Japanese representatives would be illegal and request that the meeting be held in Shanghai. Since our side has already made considerable arrangements for the Hangzhou venue and Shanghai is a concession and does not have a suitable location, most representatives do not agree. Our side is currently discussing this matter, and after a decision is made, an affairs meeting will be convened. As for Mr. Green, the chairman of the institute, he said that three Japanese representatives plan to attend, referring to attending the affairs meeting.

Fire at a Hardware Store on Route Foch

Losses Estimated at Over 10,000 Yuan

At 6:55 PM last night, a fire broke out at the Xiehe Tram Hardware Store at No. 331 Route Foch in the French Concession, due to carelessness with gasoline. In an instant, the fire spread to the neighboring Jinlongchang Hardware Store at No. 333 and Youli Woodworking Shop at No. 329. The fire brigades from various sections rushed to the scene after receiving the alarm and tried their best to put out the fire. It was not until 8:25 PM that the fire was extinguished. A total of three buildings were destroyed, along with a large quantity of goods. However, the Xiehe store, where the fire originated, suffered losses of car tires, machinery, gasoline, etc., amounting to over 10,000 yuan.

Lost Apprentice Awaiting Pickup

At 3:40 PM yesterday, the police station of the 6th District of West Shanghai brought back a runaway apprentice who was lost in the Xiaoshadu area. When asked his name, he said his surname was unknown, his given name was Tulin, he was 13 years old, from Jiangbei, and had been in Shanghai for only four or five days. He was an apprentice at a coppersmith shop, but he did not know the shop's name or address. He said he ran away because he was beaten, which is why he got lost. The boy was wearing a new blue striped cloth short shirt, blue cloth pants, black cloth shoes, had a dark complexion, and a shaved head. He is currently being held at the police station, waiting for the owner of the coppersmith shop to come and claim him.

Reader Correspondence

News from Mr. Cao Xiangzhi (Letter to the Central Military Academy)

I have served in the education field in Nantong for several years and feel that the education authorities are discriminatory and self-serving. Ashamed to associate with them, I came to Shanghai simply dressed. With the national crisis at hand, public and private matters have angered me. Rather than endure death to seek life, I abandoned my pen to join the military. I am attaching a letter to the Central Military Academy. If you believe it will be beneficial to the people's hearts, please publish it. "Letter to the Central Military Academy" Respectfully, the enemy troops have invaded our borders and penetrated deep, and the extent is still unknown. Our country's standing army is only this number, and there are no reserves. The people have no training and it is even more difficult to mobilize them in a hurry. Although our compatriots have a sincere desire to serve the country, they certainly have no effect on repelling the enemy with righteous indignation. The other day, the newspaper reported on the plan for a special military training class at your academy. This is indeed one of the emergency measures. On the one hand, it is storing up talent for the country, and on the other hand, it is cherishing talent for the country ("Bloody men will not snipe at people or commit suicide, but will have a place to belong.") It can also revitalize the superficial and boastful national spirit and expand the spirit of strict discipline. Even if the situation stabilizes and there is no need for war, it is still an essential plan for governing the country to train the people militarily. This is what Xiangzhi bows his head nine times to ask for the early realization of. Moreover, history tells us that people like Wu Zixu and Yue Goujian must have something to rely on before they can achieve something. Otherwise, people like Wen Tianxiang, Lu Xiufu, and Shi Kefa can only sacrifice themselves for righteousness and leave only memorials for future generations to mourn. Furthermore, if a country is to stand, it must gather the elites of the whole country and accumulate strength to become strong before it can achieve anything. Recently, Feng Yong University is like an osprey that cries out once. However, how much can it fly with bows and arrows filling the market? The generals in the Northeast were also not weak, but the situation was such that they could not resist and could only endure humiliation and resentment. Now, the central government still has time to respond to emergencies, and Japan has not yet reached the strength to swallow an elephant. If Japan gains Manchuria and Mongolia and has another ten years, we will certainly be ghosts under their knives, and even if the great powers want to compete with dogs for food, there will be nothing we can do. This is what Xiangzhi has deeply considered repeatedly, and I am extremely willing to go to your academy to study and take the opportunity to serve the country. Xiangzhi is thirty-one years old and graduated from Great China University. I have also been engaged in education for four years. I deeply believe that the people's morals have declined and the national spirit is waning. Educators are greedy for quick success, eager for practical benefits, and promote favoritism, and there is no righteousness at all. Therefore, Xiangzhi is extremely willing to work hard to revitalize the outlook of a county or a village. At this time, only if everyone competes with all their strength, is firm and calm, and enables the whole country to transcend national hatred, can we save the fate of the country and plan the final miraculous feat with the determination to die. This is all. I express my urgent words, with ink and tears together, and cannot fully express what I want to say.

(Reply) Your letter is extremely pertinent and extremely painful. We will publish it immediately.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory predicted at 4:30 PM yesterday that the Yangtze River basin would be cloudy and cooler, the Shandong coast would be cloudy and rainy, and there would be strong northerly winds in the Yellow Sea and the coast here. Southwest of Ogasawara, the weather is bad due to a hurricane moving northeast. There is also a hurricane west of Guam, which will move northwest. The center of the hurricane was about 120 miles within 22 degrees north latitude and 129 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, and 120 miles within 15 degrees north latitude and 139 degrees east longitude. Also, the highest temperature in this city within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 86.0 and the lowest was 68.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 81.1 and the lowest was 53.6.

Free Talk

Heartbreaking Words

— Juan

Dear compatriots. Since the tyrannical sun suddenly occupied the Northeast, launching an undeclared war, our country has retreated without resistance, without fighting back. Counting on our fingers, it has been twenty days already. Although the League of Nations has sent a note to the tyrannical sun asking them to withdraw their troops, their troops have not withdrawn and have instead occupied Yingkou and Niuzhuang, and are further demonstrating their power on the sea with warships. Step by step, they are pressing closer. On our country's side, apart from the enthusiastic patriotic students and merchants who are running around calling for national salvation, we are still at a loss. We, the masses who have no axes to grind, can only face this difficult and arduous situation with a calm and resolute attitude. We unanimously request the authorities to abolish the policy of non-resistance and to develop a spirit of fearlessness.

Removing Garden Grass, Zhaifu Talking About the Essence

Military Advisors of New and Old China

Since China is a democratic country, the common people are simply being impolite in acting as Liu Shan. However, if Liu Shan does not have Zhuge Liang, the country will be destroyed. Who is our Zhuge Liang? Where is he? If I announce his name, everyone will surely laugh until their stomachs hurt. Who do you say is the military advisor who holds the highest authority in China today? The spirit mediums, fortune tellers, physiognomists, diviners, and character analysts, and the divination tubes in front of the wooden Bodhisattva. The great men and gentlemen determine their careers based on their birthdates. Those in power use people based on their physiognomy. A criminal court prosecutor said to me: "His fierce appearance will kill people." One day, I passed by a character analysis stall and saw a female student divining there. I thought to myself: "Do female students also believe in divination?" Curiosity made me stop. The female student said: "A friend of mine hasn't written for several days. I want to ask what day I will receive a letter." The character analyst said: "Boyfriend or girlfriend?" The female student was embarrassed (I resented myself for being a thorn in her side) and only said: "Anyone will do, as long as it's a friend." When the March 18th Massacre occurred, several officials of the Provisional Government had to perform divination first before daring to attend the State Council meeting. Needless to say for the old women, whether it's marriage, travel, or illness, they all have to consult a fortune teller or a clay or wooden Bodhisattva. You always think that robbers and bandits are fearless of heaven and earth, but little do you know that they can't do without the Bodhisattva. Before the Taibao Ashu case, they had to burn incense and seek divination. If it was auspicious, they would proceed; if it was not auspicious, they would stop. This matter reminded me of Li Chuang. After Li Chuang escaped from Zhang Xianzhong, he was defeated by He Renlong. One of his subordinates, Liu Zongmin, who had previously been a blacksmith, wanted to surrender. Li Chuang found out and sat with Zongmin in a temple to sigh. He said, "People say I have the fortune to be an emperor. Why don't we ask the Bodhisattva? If it's auspicious, follow me; if it's inauspicious, take my head and surrender." Zongmin agreed and put the knife in his waist to watch. All three times were auspicious. Zongmin then killed two wives and continued to follow Li Chuang. Li Chuang then fought all the way to Beijing. There are still many Li Chuangs in China today, and Liu Zongmins are not few either. In short, in one sentence, the military advisor of old China is the god of superstition! In the scientific world of the twentieth century, a nation that worships the god of superstition as its military advisor will inevitably be eliminated by nature. Liu Shan, Liu Shan, four hundred million Liu Shans! You must quickly invite Zhuge Liang out. Who is Zhuge Liang? Three cobblers are worth one Zhuge Liang. Our three cobblers are: (1) civil officials who are not greedy for money; (2) military officers who are not afraid of death; (3) scholars who use both their hands and brains (Science, that is, science scholars.)

World Small Notes

Gandhi Salt Bottles Popular in France Gandhi, the leader of the Indian people's movement, used non-violent resistance against England to strive for the lifting of the salt ban and allow the Indian people to freely make salt on the seashore. His name shook the world. A certain porcelain factory in Paris, the capital of France, specially manufactured a kind of Gandhi salt bottle to worship the hero and provide seasoning during meals. The entire salt bottle is a small statue of Gandhi, imitating his usual squatting posture. Many small holes are opened in the head to allow salt to be sprinkled out. The gentlemen and ladies of Paris like to use this small salt bottle, which is fresh in design and exquisitely crafted. Therefore, the sales are extremely good. Some people may misunderstand and think that Gandhi's image was made into a salt bottle because he strived to lift the salt ban, which seems to contain a joking meaning. In fact, there is no such intention. Westerners worship heroes and often express it in these small things. In recent years, both England and France have indeed popularized this kind of five-flavor bottle decorated with political figures. For example, the great British politician Baldwin has also had his image made into a small wine jug by porcelain merchants in his own country.

A Talk About the Past and Present of Foreign Attitudes

— Yi Jun

The East Province has been occupied by the Japanese army for twenty days. There has been no progress in negotiations. If this continues, the country will no longer be a country. Our central government, regarding this serious problem, does not know how it will be properly resolved. People today often say that the foreign policy of the Qing Dynasty was weak and made concessions at every turn.

However, I accidentally found a passage about foreign policy in an old book about the Gengzi Rebellion during the late Qing Dynasty. Although they also knew that it was difficult to put into practice at the time, they still felt more excited than the current attitude towards foreign countries. I extracted the original text as follows:

"Edict issued on the nineteenth day of the tenth month of the twenty-fifth year of Guangxu. The current situation is difficult, and the countries are watching with covetous eyes, competing to enter my house and chambers. In terms of China's current financial and military strength, there is absolutely no reason to start a dispute. However, the arrival of the incident is really forcing us to be here. In the event that a strong enemy bullies us, threatening us with something that cannot be agreed to, we can only be justified and righteous, and fight the enemy with the same hatred. The outcome of the victory or defeat is unpredictable. The governors and governors of the provinces often have a word 'peace' in their hearts when dealing with foreign affairs, which leads to no preparation at all in temporary times. Such stubborn habits are the worst of ingratitude and betrayal of the country. This is especially strict rebuke. In the future, if there is a matter that cannot be resolved without war, if war has already been declared, there is absolutely no reason to negotiate peace immediately. The governors and governors of the provinces must work together with one heart and one mind, regardless of barriers, to supervise the generals and soldiers to kill the enemy and achieve results. The word 'peace' must not only not be spoken, but also not be kept in the heart. China has a vast territory and abundant resources, with hundreds of thousands of miles and hundreds of millions of people. If we can all be loyal to the emperor and love the country, then what strong enemy is to be feared? It is not necessary to turn swords into plowshares and rely solely on diplomatic negotiations. This is to inform you of this notice. Respect this."

Records of Scenes in the Old Capital

— Zhu An

Paper Hanger

The art of paper hanger in the northern capital surpasses the four realms and is almost on par with that of the carpenter. If the residence is newly settled and is disliked for its old and broken appearance, the paper hanger is called to paper it, and it will be fresh and eye-catching. The most magical of its arts is the wellhead, which is all delimited with colored paper, which is as if it were painted in color. Wu Zi Feng, there is no trace to be found. In recent years, the price of labor has gradually increased, and each room requires three or four yuan. However, in terms of stucco work, its price is much cheaper. It is said that the Qing court needed paper hangers, and Suzhou sent four people specially. As soon as they arrived, a small gourd was issued and they were ordered to paper it. One person meditated for a long time, and then removed the stems and placed them in a bowl to sharpen them. The three people shook each other, making them extremely smooth. Then, soak the white cotton paper in water overnight, mix it evenly, and pour it in. That is, pour it away. Wait for it to dry and then pour it. After doing this several times, advance to the emperor. Breaking it reveals that there is paper throughout, with no traces of patching. Perhaps this technique was transmitted from Wu to the Northern Capital. In the past generations, the capital cities were the gathering places for famous craftsmen, while their hometowns may have lost the tradition. The ceiling is the most difficult part of papering the house. On top of the house, sorghum is used as a frame. The reeds are tied upside down on the rafters, and paper is pasted under them, which is called a ceiling. Those who are not good at papering will often wrinkle. There is no such thing as a craftsman in the Northern Capital. Extravagant people arrange them in squares like caisson. Recently, there have been people who use palm curtains as ceilings, which are also quite elegant. However, the method of papering cannot last for long. Rats nest in it, and they will wear it out in a few months. It is also easy to get dirty when touched by hand, so it must be changed every one or two years. The art of architecture is advancing day by day, and this art will eventually be eliminated.

The windows in the north are tall and large. The lower layer is mostly embedded with glass, and the upper layer is pasted with Goryeo paper to prevent wind and sand. In summer, they are pasted with green cold cloth, and paper is used as a curtain, which is covered on it, and can be stretched and rolled at any time. The shape is elegant and clean, and the value is also cheap.

Ink is a Benevolent Drink. Wang Shizi titled Cloud. Floods raged in China. The people are in pain and leaving. How can vegetable roots be obtained? All the trees have no bark. The rest, such as the preparatory members of the association, Ms. Yu and Ms. Tang, also have several exquisite works of their own. It is said that no tickets will be used for the meeting. At that time, it can be imagined that the number of visitors will be like a tide. (Transfer remuneration to help relief)

An Unprecedented New Record

— Chang Tian

The world record for the 100-meter dash is, at best, just over nine seconds. Its slow progress is truly imaginable. However, looking back at the industries of Europe and the United States, managed with scientific methods, the speed of various manufactured products has greatly increased, almost everything exceeding its former rate by half. The inability of human power to compete with machines is further proven here.

Among the advancements in work speed, the two clothing-making competitions that caused a sensation in England are most noteworthy. The first was held in Leeds, specifically for Minister Shaw-Lefevre. From shearing wool off a sheep to the completion of a garment ready to wear, it only took three hours and twenty and a half minutes. However, the second time, at the Crolles company on Minories Street, they made a similar garment, breaking the record in one hour and ten minutes. The shearing of the sheep for that garment started at 10:25 a.m., and it was ready to be worn to a banquet before lunchtime.

It is also said that the pair of leather shoes worn by Minister Shaw-Lefevre were made in a similar rushed manner. From the removal of the animal hide to the completion of the shoes, it took thirty and a half minutes. However, the old American record was only twenty minutes. By comparison, it is quite inadequate.

Aside from industry, the rush system has recently been applied to agricultural products. It is remembered that in 1899, Mr. Blount of Birmingham, England, used fresh barley, reaped, threshed, ground, and made bread in eight hours. By 1906, after painstaking research, he had shortened the time to three and a half hours. However, in the summer of 1911, he redoubled his efforts to break his own record. He planted some wheat in a certain place, and on the afternoon of August 7th of that year, at 2:35 p.m., he began reaping. First, he threshed the wheat by hand, then ground it with a machine. After one hour and forty-two minutes, the flour was mixed with yeast and placed in the bread oven. The bread was baked in only two hours and twenty-one minutes. The record was broken once again.

It is also remembered that in 1878, a certain British engineer used the rush system to build a locomotive engine in twenty-five hours and thirty minutes. The Pennsylvania Railroad Company of the United States, upon hearing this news, was greatly surprised. They also wanted to compete with him in the same way. The result was reduced to seventeen hours. However, twenty years later, in 1899, the Great Eastern Railway Company of England, to save face for the British, used eighty-eight workers to prepare to build the same engine. Work began at 9:08 a.m. on December 10th of that year. In just nine hours and forty-seven minutes, the entire engine was completed. Wouldn't you call that amazing?

Speaking Department Rotary Club

The Pestle of Knocking Dreams (8)

— Cheng Zhanlu

Pei Shi's ideal was not wrong! In this century, the Englishman Stephenson had already invented the method of running trains on railroads. His thinking and Pei Shi's were the same, truly echoing the ancient saying, "Sages will emerge from the Northern and Southern Seas, with the same heart." However, Stephenson was born in England and invented mechanical work, enough for people to admire, imitate, improve, and publicize. Pei Shi was born in China and invented mechanical work, only earning himself nicknames like "fool," "idiot," and "old simpleton"!

"Pei Shi is dead! Pei Shi hanged himself!" Initially, there were voices of astonishment and lamentation in society.

"Pei Shi's death is pitiful but not regrettable!" Gradually, society's opinion changed.

"Old Man Pei was not wrong, the mistake was with Pei Chi; if he didn't die, who would?" Society's final opinion was to unanimously condemn the already deceased Pei Shi.

Why did Pei Shi die? He died under the examination system! He also died under the censorship of public opinion! He also died under the tyranny of his family! He also died under the poisonous hands of those who opposed scientific thought! The Stephenson of the East, vanished like a fleeting flower! Alas!

The cause of death:! Tao Chi and Pei Shi went to take the exam together. Tao Chi passed and became a Xiucai (a successful candidate in the imperial examination), but Pei Shi was nowhere on the list. Although Xiucai was a small title, in the 18th century, because of the saying "A Xiucai is the root of a prime minister," it gained extraordinary importance in society. Once the results were announced, the gains and losses were clear, and laughter and tears naturally arose together. Upon seeing his name not on the list, Pei Shi did not feel any particular gain or loss. Not passing the Xiucai exam could save him all the future trouble of the annual and provincial exams. He ran home in one breath, not busy with anything else, but busy completing his work on a small car that could freely travel on two wires because this work was about to be finished! Who knew that this would anger Old Man Pei, anger the Old Man Pei who only knew how to tumble through the list of examination successes. He saw that his son had not passed the Xiucai exam and was already frustrated to death. Not passing the Xiucai exam and still playing with these ingenious and useless toys, violating his subjective belief of "not doing what is useless and harms what is useful," this blaze of anger began to burn vigorously! He beat his son – smashing the door latch as an instrument of corporal punishment – and burned all the works influenced by these ingenious and useless crafts! He broke, destroyed, and eliminated the car that was about to be completed and travel freely on the wires! He ordered Pei Shi to only read classical texts from now on, and only write eight-legged essays! … Poor Pei Shi! He endured silently and hanged himself!

Gold Standard Prices Plunge

News of Japan Possibly Abandoning Gold Standard

Drop Exceeds Twenty-Six Taels. Yesterday, the 7th, the price of gold plummeted. A violent tide and alarming waves of rises and falls led to great confusion. One moment the price was two or three taels down, the next, seven or eight taels. Throughout the day, the fluctuations totaled twenty-five or twenty-six taels, which was considered enormous. The psychology of those in the trade was especially perplexed. The imbalance between supply and demand was probably due to a slight drop in overseas silver prices, and also because of renewed proposals in the United States to rescue the silver market. Confidence waned, but speculators remained brave. The market opened low, already breaking 710 taels. The exchange rate was complex, with British gold soft and American gold hard. Many in the trade were selling. Later, when banks did not follow suit to buy, the market seemed to ease. Furthermore, front-line operators were actively hedging, causing the price to rise again. Suddenly, news spread that Japan was considering abandoning the gold standard, banning the export of cash gold, and that there were significant disputes within the cabinet. This deteriorated the market atmosphere, causing a major panic. Sellers became bold, suddenly breaking the 700-tael mark. It was Wednesday, and there was no foreign exchange market, but this dramatic change was unexpected.

Early Market Shakes and Fails. The market opened in the morning already down four taels at 720 taels. The broad silver bar fell three-eighths, the forward rate seven-sixteenths, and the silver price fell only one-eighth. Another tael was lost, but some buyers appeared, pushing the price up to 21 taels. Then, due to British gold loosening, banks were mutually trading this month at 1.7375, then 4.375. Yarn and Cotton Yarn Market Buying Sentiment Stronger

The yarn market has turned firm, and the trend is rising again. As foreign cotton has rebounded, and rumors have calmed down, the market is more stable. Buying sentiment in the market is stronger, but actual yarn business is still flat. However, there are rumors that Japanese factories may be stopping production, so there are quite a few speculators buying in, and the market is rising.

Human Label Price Up Two Taels: The human label price opened in the morning. Due to the rebound in foreign cotton, the market atmosphere was tighter, and sellers were scarce. The price for each month rose by 1.78 qian to 2.1 qian. The price fell by nearly 5 qian in the afternoon, and rose by 3 qian in the long-term. The total transaction volume was 61,400 bales. The sales were: Tong Yu 1,150 bales, Tai Xing 2,700 bales, Yi Yu 2,850 bales, Da Chang 2,000 bales, Tian Cheng 1,000 bales, Tai Chang 1,000 bales, and Yi Chang 3,400 bales. The purchases were: Ji Feng 2,600 bales, Gong Tai 3,000 bales, Rong Xing 2,400 bales, Geng Feng 4,900 bales, and Chang Feng 3,900 bales. The closing prices are recorded on the left.

Actual Goods Ordinary: The actual yarn sales are still good. According to the statistics, all guilds bought a total of 920 bales, and peers bought 130 bales. The market is ordinary. Customers from Guangdong bought 280 bales, customers from the mainland bought 70 bales, customers from Sichuan bought 300 bales, customers from Jiangxi bought 130 bales, customers from Changsha bought 50 bales, and Shuangbang bought 90 bales.

Cotton Market Has a Violent Reaction

The cotton market has a sharp rise. Because American cotton has risen, the market is tight again. Bulls are buying in and adding positions. Most people expect American cotton to have an active rise. Buyers are even more active. However, American cotton production has increased more, and sales are not booming. Therefore, large speculators are still short selling when prices rise. Furthermore, the difference in foreign cotton prices is still low by 8 to 9 taels.

Han Label Rebounds by One Taels: The exchange's Han label opened in the morning. Because American cotton had risen, and the market atmosphere was tight, the price rose by 8 or 9 qian. In the afternoon, the near month rose by another 2 or 3 qian, and the distant month was flat. The total transaction volume for the day was 187,500 dan. The sales were: Mei Ji 3,500 dan, Zhen Da 3,700 dan, Yi Cheng 4,700 dan, Yu Da 4,600 dan, Xin Cheng 5,800 dan, and Chang Yu 2,100 dan. The purchases were: Ji Feng 6,800 dan, Gong Tai 6,100 dan, Tian Long 3,600 dan, Geng Feng 6,300 dan, and Yi Yu 3,100 dan. The closing prices are recorded on the left.

American Cotton Rebounds Over Thirty Pounds

Yesterday, American cotton, due to the strength of Wall Street, made a reactive purchase. Shorts were covering, and the market was active and firm. Futures rose 31 to 35 pounds, and spot rose 35 pounds. British cotton futures rose 3 to 4 points, and spot fell 24 points. Egyptian cotton spot fell 30 points. The Indian cotton market was flat. Pingor fell 2.5 rupees, Aumra fell 3.25 rupees, and Baloqi fell 2.25 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (6th wire):

Private Estimate of American Cotton

A 6th New York wire said that the American Cotton Collection Office's estimate of this year's new cotton is 68.1% of the normal annual production, totaling 16,004,000 bales, an increase of 501,000 bales compared to the previous estimate (September 4th). The cotton already ginned is 5,181,000 bales. Also, the average estimated quantity of the brokers at the New York Stock Exchange is 15,960,000 bales, an increase of 388,000 bales compared to the previous estimate (September 1st).

Grain Market at Hexia Slightly Firm

Nantou: Yesterday, Chang, Xi, Su, and Tong sold over a dozen batches of early rice. Merchants in Hexia insisted on higher prices, refusing to sell unless prices increased. Furthermore, the prices in production areas like Beitan and Pingwang differed from Shanghai prices by as much as 30 cents. Given this situation and the unfavorable weather, although sales were not brisk, the market shape had become firm. Only three batches of Qingjiao new foreign Du Jian and new early rice were seen. While the outflow was weak, prices saw a slight softening.

Xinzha: Yesterday's arrivals were not abundant, with a few batches of thick early rice arriving. Local merchants' sales were lively, and the outflow of processed rice saw a price increase of a few cents. New early rice was broken, and local shops were extremely indifferent, reducing the price by 40-50 cents. New foreign Lu Jian and Jiaobai Jian were firm. A large amount of glutinous rice and early rice arrived, but the outflow was limited, and the price also fell by 10-20 cents.

Turnaround in Foreign Rice Sales

Northern Merchants Continue to Handle Spot Goods

Inland Merchants Inquire About Futures

The foreign rice market had been declining due to continuous dumping by foreign firms, and sales had disappeared in various regions. The market seemed to be in a state of collapse. The market atmosphere had been very poor in recent days, with some predicting that small Jiaomi would fall to 8 or 9 yuan. However, yesterday, foreign firms stopped dumping, and none of them received telegrams to continue selling. Therefore, no new transactions were made for package deals. Spot goods were still being handled by Northern merchants from Tianjin and other regions. Inland merchants were also inquiring about futures. Although prices had not risen sharply, the market had become more lively. A transaction for 300 bags of Saigon spot rice was made at 12.2 yuan. Over a thousand bags of small Jiaomi were sold at 10.06 to 10.03 yuan. Futures trading saw 800 tons of March rice at 5.15 to 5.25 taels, 100 tons of October rice at 5.045 taels, and 100 tons of November rice at 5.135 taels. The prices for October and November were slightly lower, while the price for March at 5.25 taels was higher by 8 points.

Sharp Decline in Flour and Wheat After Noon

Russian Wheat Prices Dropped for Sale: Yesterday, the wheat market was greatly shaken because the first batch of American wheat had already been tendered for the remaining amount, and the second and third batches were arriving in Shanghai soon. Furthermore, Russian wheat prices dropped for sale, with telegrams reporting only 3.3 taels. As a result, the market was greatly shaken. The market opened in the afternoon with a sudden and dramatic change. The closing price for the current month decreased by 8 points, the next month by 1.1 cents, December by 1.3 cents, January and March by 9 points each, and February by 1.1 cents. There was no market for spot goods, and the future looked bleak.

Flour Turned from Rise to Fall: Yesterday, the flour market was affected by wheat, turning from a rise to a fall. When the market opened in the morning, prices for all months rose by several points to half a cent due to the outflow to Northern regions and short covering. In the afternoon, wheat futures saw a sharp decline, and manufacturers took the opportunity to increase their positions. New shorts competed with longs, leading to a market decline that could not be contained. The final closing price fell by 2-3 points for both near and distant months. However, the quoted price for foreign wheat rose by 40-50 cents.

Sugar Market: 4,000 Bags of Coarse and White Sugar Sold

Heavy Trading in Dumped Goods

Yesterday's sugar market telegrams reported Cuban spot sugar at 1.4375, New York sugar futures for December at 1.40, March of next year at 1.36, up 2 points from previous telegrams. May was at 1.40, up 1 point, and September was at 1.48, also up 2 points. Java spot and futures sugar remained unchanged. According to the association's quotations, Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse white transactions were still scarce, with inventory white sugar at 11.35 to 11.4 taels per bag, new sugar at 10.5 taels, No. 20 medium white sugar at 10.09 taels, and soft Dutch white sugar at 12.05 taels. The market was firm. Taikoo Sugar HM brand was at 11.75 taels, with few sales at the door. Buying interest was quite strong, and the trend was very good. the brand was at 12.3 taels. The market was relatively flat. Zhenxiang sold 4,000 bags of old coarse white sugar at 11 taels. The market was very quick. As for dumped Dutch sugar, Nanshenglong sold 300 tons of old packed coarse white sugar for October and November shipment at a price of 5.55 Dutch guilders. Dachang sold 500 tons of No. 16 medium coarse white sugar for November and December shipment at 5.3 guilders. The bank's intention was still strong, and all were sold. The market shape was still clever.

North-South Goods: Hunan Lotus Seeds and White Lotus Seeds Have Both Eased

Recently, Hunan lotus seeds have become sluggish in various markets, and market prices have fallen by 2-3 taels before and after. Prices in the Hankou market have also eased. According to letters, the price per load is 37 to 36.6 taels. The current market price here for Hengzhou shipments is 61-62 taels, and Changde lotus seeds are 60 taels. Merchants from Ningbo and Guangzhou are purchasing in small quantities, with other merchants making only scattered purchases. The land price for white lotus seeds is 64 yuan, and the Shanghai market price is 52-53 taels. Guangzhou merchants have a few transactions, but the rest are limited. The market outlook is flat.

Silk and Tea: Gongxi Green Tea Has Slight Movement in Russian Sales

Yesterday, the local foreign firms in the tea market. The Russian Aid Society's foreign firm resumed handling Gongxi green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi. Baitou, Zhuang, Yulong, Qianyi, and other firms also slightly increased their inventory. However, the selling price was reduced to 40-50 taels, which was 3-4 taels lower than before. English firms had some outflow for needle-shaped and eyebrow-shaped green tea. The market situation has not improved. Sales of other green teas such as Zhenmei and Xiami, as well as Qining black tea, remained sluggish.

Hardware: Qingdao Merchants Telegram to Stop Handling Hardware

Since the violent Japanese occupation of the three northeastern provinces, commercial activity there has ceased. Recently, there have been reports of unrest in Qingdao. Therefore, yesterday, XX and other firms from Qingdao received telegrams from the Qingdao headquarters to stop handling goods, reducing another outlet for hardware. Fortunately, transactions by the Tianjin and Yantai merchants have been relatively active recently, resulting in a total transaction volume of over 3-4 thousand loads. Furthermore, the Hankou merchants have also been doing reasonably well recently. Yesterday, over 400 boxes of tinplate were sold at 14 taels. 200-300 loads each of black iron sheet and white iron sheet were also sold. The merchants also had a very strong appetite for grooved steel and English steel plates. Because of the small amount of existing stock and good demand from various regions, the market outlook for new lead wire is very optimistic. In addition, French-West nails, large lead bars, and angle iron also had some sales. However, the price fluctuations were very slight.

Piece Goods: New Clothing Merchants Buying Wool Fabrics

Recently, the market for wool fabrics has been very stable. Yesterday, various calling shops (i.e., new clothing merchants) on this street, such as shops in Hongkou, Shilu, Nanshi, and Caishi Street, started purchasing. Yuan Chang blue-gray plain broadcloth, mixed color, miscellaneous color, plaid Walter cloth, yuan qing zhigong cloth, riding breeches cloth, and chocolate cloth all had transactions. Whole boxes were shipped with stamped tickets, and individual pieces were stamped and sold on credit.

Business News

The Dashin Silk and Satin Bureau, located at the corner of Sanma Road in Shilu, announces that since the construction of a new five-story building and the expansion of business, it has been a week. A large-scale clearance sale of twenty-five days has been held since the 22nd of last month. Business has been unusually crowded in recent days. The newly arrived goods are unique in color and design, and the prices are low. The general public is scrambling to purchase them. At this time of golden autumn, it is the day for all walks of life to make new clothes. Please do not miss the opportunity. Furthermore, anyone who purchases materials from the bureau, regardless of the amount, will receive a free copy of a one-week commemorative special issue. Both the photos and the text inside are exquisite, and the cost is more than half a yuan, etc.

Dahua Optical Company announces that the company has been located at the old North Gate for many years. The glasses made are accurate in optical power. Now, due to the increasing prosperity of the business and the inadequacy of the original site, and for the convenience of customers in the northern city, it has moved to the north end of Yokohama Bridge on North Sichuan Road and is scheduled to officially open on October 5. During the opening period, a large-scale clearance sale will be held, and commemorative glasses will be sold at a price of only two yuan per pair, with a limit of one pair per person, etc.
